 <BODY BGCOLOR="WHITE">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times 
New Roman" ALIGN="right"><B>Exhibit 10.1 </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times 
New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B><U>AMENDED AND RESTATED EXECUTIVE EMPLOYMENT 
AGREEMENT </U></B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; 
font-family:Times New Roman">THIS AMENDED AND RESTATED EXECUTIVE EMPLOYMENT 
AGREEMENT (the &#147;<U>Agreement</U>&#148;), effective as of the Effective Date
(as defined
below), is entered into by and between SAExploration Holdings, Inc., a Delaware 
corporation (the &#147;<U>Employer</U>&#148; or the &#147;<U>Company</U>&#148;),
and <U>Jeff Hastings</U>, an individual residing in the Province of British 
Columbia,
Canada (the &#147;<U>Executive</U>&#148;) and amends, restates and replaces in 
its entirety the Executive Employment Agreement dated as of June&nbsp;24, 2013, 
other than the provisions of the Non-Disclosure Agreement (as such term is 
defined herein)
(the &#147;<U>Original Employment Agreement</U>&#148;). The Employer and the 
Executive may be referred to singularly as &#147;<U>Party</U>&#148; or 
collectively as &#147;<U>Parties</U>.&#148; Unless otherwise specified, 
capitalized terms have the
meanings set forth herein. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:24pt; margin-bottom:0pt;
font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><U>RECITALS </U></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; 
font-family:Times New Roman">WHEREAS, the Company and certain of its 
subsidiaries and such other parties identified therein entered into that certain
Restructuring Support
Agreement dated as of June&nbsp;13, 2016, whereby the parties thereto have 
agreed to enter into certain transactions that will have the effect of 
restructuring and recapitalizing the Company (the &#147;<U>RSA</U>&#148;) 
effective upon the Closing
Date (as such term is defined in the RSA); </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; 
margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New 
Roman">WHEREAS, prior to the Effective Date, the Employer has employed the 
Executive as the Executive
Chairman of the Board; </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-
indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">WHEREAS, in connection 
with and pursuant to the provisions of the RSA, the Parties have agreed to amend
the
Original Employment Agreement on the terms and conditions contained herein 
effective immediately upon the date of approval (the &#147;<U>Effective 
Date</U>&#148;) by the Board of Directors of the Company (the 
&#147;<U>Board</U>&#148;); </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; 
font-family:Times New Roman">WHEREAS, effective immediately upon the Effective 
Date, the Company will employ the Executive as the Chief Executive Officer and 
Chairman of
the Board, and the Executive desires to be employed by the Employer on the terms
and conditions contained herein; </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-
bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New 
Roman">WHEREAS, the Employer
acknowledges and rewards the value and loyalty of the Executive and seeks to 
build and protect the Company&#146;s stability, growth, customer base, 
technology and other competitive advantages; and </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; 
font-family:Times New Roman">WHEREAS, the Executive wishes to evidence his 
commitment to the Company and its objectives. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; 
font-family:Times New Roman">NOW, THEREFORE, in consideration of the foregoing 
premises and the respective agreements hereinafter set forth and the mutual 
benefits to be
derived hereinafter, the Employer and the Executive hereby agree as follows: 
</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:24pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-
family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><U>AGREEMENTS </U></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; 
font-family:Times New Roman">1. <U>Employment Term</U>. The Employer hereby 
agrees to continue to employ the Executive commencing on the Effective Date and 
ending on the
third anniversary thereafter (the &#147;<U>Initial Term</U>&#148;); 
<U>provided</U>, <U>however</U>, that at the end of the Initial Term, the 
Executive&#146;s </P>
<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times 
New Roman">
employment and this Agreement shall automatically renew or extend for 
consecutive terms of one (1)&nbsp;year on each succeeding anniversary of the 
Effective Date (each such renewal or extension a
&#147;<U>Renewal Term</U>&#148;), unless either Party gives prior written notice
to the other Party of its desire to terminate the Agreement at least 90 days 
prior to the expiration of the Initial Term or any Renewal Term, as applicable 
(the Initial
Term and each Renewal Term, collectively, the &#147;<U>Term</U>&#148;). 
Notwithstanding the foregoing, the Parties shall have the termination rights as 
set forth in Section&nbsp;5 of this Agreement. Termination of this Agreement for
any reason
whatsoever by any Party shall have no effect on the continued enforceability of 
any ancillary agreement, specifically including the Non-Disclosure Agreement 
executed by the Executive in favor of the Employer concurrently with the 
Original Employment
Agreement, (the &#147;<U>Non-Disclosure Agreement</U>&#148;). The obligations of
the Parties under Sections 5 through 25 herein shall survive according to the 
terms of each provision. The Executive accepts such continued employment and 
agrees to
continue to perform the services specified herein, all upon the terms and 
conditions hereinafter stated. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-
bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">2. 
<U>Duties</U>. During the
Term, the Executive shall serve in the position of Chief Executive Officer and 
Chairman of the Board and shall report to and be subject to the general 
direction and control of the Board or its designee. In such capacity he shall be
responsible for
the supervision of the day to day operations of the Company and the 
implementation of its business plans and strategies, in each case, subject to 
the Board and in accordance with and subject to budgets approved from time to 
time by such Board. The
Executive shall perform such duties consistent with the Executive&#146;s 
position, as well as other related duties from time to time assigned to the 
Executive by the Board. The Executive further agrees to perform, without 
additional compensation,
such other services for the Employer and for any of its affiliates as the Board 
shall from time to time specify, if such services are of the nature commonly 
associated with or similar to that of the Executive&#146;s position with a 
company engaged
in activities similar to the activities engaged in by the Employer at the time 
of execution of this Agreement. For purposes of the Non-Disclosure Agreement and
Sections 5 through 25 herein, the term &#147;Employer&#148; shall be deemed to 
include
and refer to any and all affiliates of the Employer. The Executive acknowledges 
and agrees that the Non-Disclosure Agreement executed simultaneously with the 
Original Employment Agreement is hereby incorporated by reference herein and 
made a part
hereof and that the Non-Disclosure Agreement constitutes a material part of this
Agreement. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; 
font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">3. <U>Extent of Service</U>. The 
Executive
shall devote his full business time, attention, and energy to the business of 
the Employer, and shall not be engaged in any other business activity that 
competes with or detracts from the business of the Employer during the Term of 
this Agreement.
The foregoing shall not be construed as preventing the Executive from making 
passive investments in other businesses or enterprises, if (i)&nbsp;such 
investments will not require services on the part of the Executive which would 
in any material way
impair the performance of his duties under this Agreement, or (ii)&nbsp;such 
other businesses or enterprises are not engaged in any business competitive with
the business of the Employer or any of its affiliates. The Executive shall be 
based in the
vicinity of the Kelowna metropolitan area (or such other area as may be agreed 
upon by the Parties) and, subject to travel requirements as reasonably necessary
to support successful business development efforts and management of the 
business, shall
perform his services from a mutually agreed location in that area. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P 
STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New 
Roman" ALIGN="right">Amended and Restated
Executive Employment Agreement </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt;
font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="right">Page 2 </P>
<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; 
font-family:Times New Roman">4. <U>Compensation and Benefits</U>. As payment for
the services to be rendered by the Executive
hereunder during the Term of this Agreement, the Executive shall be entitled to 
the following: </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-
indent:8%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(a) receive payment of 
the
Executive&#146;s annual base salary at the rate of not less than US$664,198.00 a
year (the &#147;<U>Base Salary</U>&#148;), less deductions required by law, 
payable in accordance with the Employer&#146;s standard payroll schedule, but 
not less
frequently than monthly; <U>provided</U>, that commencing with the 
Company&#146;s 2017 fiscal year, the Executive&#146;s Base Salary may be 
increased annually (but not decreased without the written consent of the 
Executive) in the discretion of the
Board; </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-
size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(b) a monthly automobile allowance of 
US$2,750.00 per month payable in accordance with the Employer&#146;s standard 
payroll
schedule, and which shall be subject to customary deductions and withholding; 
</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-
size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(c) continue to be eligible to 
participate in any
short-term and long-term incentive compensation plans, annual bonus plans and 
such other management incentive programs or arrangements of the Company approved
by the Board that are generally available to the Company&#146;s senior 
executives and
continue to be eligible to receive annual performance cash awards 
(&#147;<U>Annual Cash Awards</U>&#148;) at the rate of 50% to 150% of Base 
Salary (the &#147;<U>Target Percentage</U>&#148;), and the Executive will be 
entitled to a guaranteed 50%
annual performance cash award and as much as 150% if certain executive goals 
(the &#147;Executive Goals&#148;) are reached as identified and approved by the 
Compensation Committee of the Board (the &#147;<U>Compensation 
Committee</U>&#148;), but not
to exceed the maximum award permissible under the applicable long-term incentive
plan for such annual award; <U>provided</U>, that, at the option of the 
Compensation Committee, up to 50% of any Annual Cash Award payable to the 
Executive may be paid
in shares of the Company&#146;s common stock (which is in addition to any shares
of the Company&#146;s common stock reserved for issuance under the SAExploration
Holdings, Inc. 2016 Long-Term Incentive Plan, as may be amended, restated and
supplemented from time to time (the &#147;<U>Equity Incentive Plan</U>&#148;)); 
<U>provided</U>, <U>further</U>, that such Target Percentage will be applied to 
twelve (12)&nbsp;times the highest paid monthly base salary within the 
applicable
calendar year. Commencing with the Company&#146;s 2017 fiscal year, the 
Executive Goals will be set by the Compensation Committee under the applicable 
long-term incentive plan for such annual award but in any event shall not exceed
the maximum award
permissible under such applicable plan; </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-
bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(d) the
Executive will be entitled to participate, on the same basis generally as other 
similarly
situated employees of the Company, in all benefits as may be offered by the 
Company from time to time; </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; 
text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(e) reimbursement 
of reasonable
expenses incurred by the Executive in accordance with such expense reimbursement
policies of the Company; and </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; 
text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(f) paid vacation
of eight
(8)&nbsp;weeks per year. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; 
text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(g) <U>Equity 
Compensation</U>. The Executive shall be eligible to participate in the Equity 
Incentive Plan and
such other equity incentive programs or arrangements of the Company approved by 
the Board that are generally available to the Company&#146;s senior executives. 
The </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P 
STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New 
Roman" ALIGN="right">Amended and Restated
Executive Employment Agreement </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt;
font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="right">Page 3 </P>
<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times 
New Roman">
Board or the Compensation Committee, as applicable, pursuant to written 
corporate action taken or at a meeting held, in either case, shall, effective, 
on September&nbsp;26, 2016 (the
&#147;<U>Grant Date</U>&#148;), subject to the Executive&#146;s employment on 
such Grant Date, award to the Executive the following: </P> <P STYLE="margin-
top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:13%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times 
New Roman">(i)
<U>Stock Units</U>. 88,252 Stock Units (as such term is defined in the Equity 
Incentive Plan) under the Equity Incentive Plan (the &#147;<U>MIP RSU 
Grant</U>&#148;) pursuant to a Stock Units Agreement (as such term is defined in
the Equity Incentive
Plan) that will provide for vesting of the MIP RSU Grant in equal installments, 
subject to the Executive&#146;s continued employment, except as otherwise 
specified, as follows: </P>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-
size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="13%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">(A)</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">one-third (1/3)&nbsp;of the MIP RSU Grant on the 
earliest to occur of: (1)&nbsp;the date that occurs after the Grant Date on 
which the Company shall have received Oil and Gas Production Tax Credit 
Certificates under AS
43.55.023 or AS 43.55.025 assigned to the Company by Alaska Seismic Ventures, 
LLC and issued by the Tax Division of the State of Alaska, together with all 
such certificates received after the Closing Date, that are in an aggregate face
amount of not
less than US$25 million (the &#147;<U>Tax Credits</U>&#148;); (2)&nbsp;to the 
extent the Tax Credits have been received on or prior to the Grant Date, the 
Grant Date; or (3)&nbsp;the first anniversary of the Closing Date; 
</TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">one-third (1/3)&nbsp;of the MIP RSU Grant on the 
second anniversary of the Closing Date; and </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-

<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt;

<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; 
font-family:Times New Roman">5. <U>Termination</U>. The Executive&#146;s 
employment with the Company under this Agreement may be terminated in accordance
with this
Section&nbsp;5. The date upon which any such termination becomes effective shall
be deemed the &#147;Termination Date&#148;. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; 
margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New 
Roman">(a)
<U>Termination by the Company for Cause</U>. The Company may terminate the 
Executive&#146;s employment with the Company under this Agreement for Cause at 
any time without notice and without any payment to the Executive whatsoever, 
save and except
for the payment of any Base Salary, vacation accrued but unpaid up to the 
Termination Date and out of pocket expenses in accordance with 
Section&nbsp;4(e), if the Executive engages in any of the following conduct 
(termination for
&#147;<U>Cause</U>&#148;): </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; 
text-indent:13%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(i) the breaching 
of any material provision of this Agreement after the Company has given the 
Executive not
less than 30 days written notice of such breach and a period of not less than 30
days to correct, or cause to be corrected, such breach; </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:13%; font-size:10pt; 
font-family:Times New Roman">(ii) knowing and intentional misappropriation of 
funds or property of the Company or its affiliates; </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:13%; font-size:10pt; 
font-family:Times New Roman">(iii) engaging in conduct, even if not in 
connection with the performance of the duties hereunder, which might be 
reasonably expected to
result in any effect materially adverse to the interests of the Company or any 
of its affiliates, such as fraud, dishonesty, conviction (or a judicial finding 
of evidence sufficient to convict) of any felony; </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P 
STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:13%; font-size:10pt;

assigned to the Executive in accordance with the
terms herein after the Company has given the Executive not less than 15 days 
written notice of such failure and a period of not less than 15 days to correct,
or cause to be corrected, such failure; and </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:13%; font-size:10pt;

the Company or any of its affiliates that are promulgated from time to time by 
the Company,
<U>provided</U>, <U>however</U>, that the Company shall not be unreasonably 
arbitrary in its enforcement of corporate policies with respect to the 
Executive. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; 
font-family:Times New Roman">(b) <U>Termination by the Executive for Good 
Reason</U>. The Executive shall have good reason (&#147;<U>Good 
Reason</U>&#148;) as defined
below to resign his employment within sixty (60)&nbsp;days following notice and 
receive the same payments as provided under Section&nbsp;5(d) (and subject to 
the same release requirement), provided the Executive has first provided written
notice to
the Employer of conduct warranting termination of the Executive&#146;s 
employment for Good Reason and provided the Employer a period of not less than 
thirty (30)&nbsp;days to cure such conduct, without the written consent of the 
Executive: </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:13%; font-size:10pt; 
font-family:Times New Roman">(i) a material diminution in the nature and scope 
of the Executive&#146;s authorities or duties, including but not limited to a 
change in the
Executive&#146;s reporting relationship, a required move of more than a 50-mile 
radius of the Executive&#146;s employment prior to any such relocation, except 
for reasonably required travel on the Company&#146;s business, a reduction in 
pay (which
shall not be triggered by the Company&#146;s setting of the Executive Goals, 
beginning with the Company&#146;s 2017 fiscal year, pursuant Section&nbsp;4(c) 
above, even if the Executive&#146;s Annual Cash Award payout decreases as a 
result) or
removal from the Company&#146;s Board of Directors; or </P> <P STYLE="margin-
top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:13%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times 
New Roman">(ii) a material breach of this Agreement by the Employer. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; 
font-family:Times New Roman">(c) <U>Termination by the Executive Without Good 
Reason</U>. The Executive may terminate his employment with the Company at any 
time, for any
reason, by providing 60 days&#146; advance written notice to the Company, which 
may be waived in whole or in part by the Company. If the Company waives the 
notice period in whole or in part, the Company shall pay the Base Salary for the
portion of
the notice period that has been waived. The Executive shall only be entitled to 
payment of any accrued but unpaid Base Salary, accrued but unpaid out of pocket 
expenses in accordance with Section&nbsp;4(e) hereof and vacation pay accrued 
but unpaid
up to the Termination Date. The Executive shall not be entitled to any accrued 
annual bonus or other benefits. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-
bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(d) 
<U>Termination by the
Company Without Cause</U>. The Company may terminate the Executive&#146;s 
employment, without Cause as defined in Sections 5(a), in which case the Company
shall pay the Executive the following, less withholdings required by law: </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:13%; font-size:10pt; 
font-family:Times New Roman">(i) all accrued but unpaid Base Salary to the 
Termination Date; </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:13%; font-size:10pt;

Termination Date; </P>

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:13%; font-size:10pt;

(2)&nbsp;years&#146; bonuses paid to the Executive, plus

in an amount as provided under the applicable bonus plan of the Company,

<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:13%; font-size:10pt;

eligible to receive such reimbursement until the earliest of (x)&nbsp;the 18 
month
anniversary of the Termination Date; (y)&nbsp;the date the Executive is no 
longer eligible to receive COBRA continuation coverage; and (z)&nbsp;the date on
which the Executive becomes eligible to receive substantially similar coverage 
from another
employer; and </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-

any provision of any outstanding equity award agreement that might otherwise be

immediate acceleration of all unvested equity awards granted under the Equity 
Incentive Plan or any other equity incentive plan or long-term incentive plan of
the Company, such that all outstanding unvested equity awards which have not 
already
vested, shall immediately vest as of the Termination Date. </P> <P 
STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New

Section&nbsp;5(d) (other than

Company not later than fifty-two (52)&nbsp;days following the Termination Date.

<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt;

not later than fifty-two (52)&nbsp;days after the Termination Date subject to

shall not be subject to the requirement of mitigation, nor reduced by any actual
mitigation by the Executive. The right to receive any of the above payments 
shall be forfeited if the required full and final release has not been received 
before the

begins in one taxable year and ends in a second taxable year, the payment date 
shall be deemed to be the later of (i)&nbsp;the first business day in the year 
following
the year in which the Executive&#146;s &#147;separation from service&#148; 
occurs or (ii)&nbsp;the last day of such 52-day period. The payments referred to
in Section&nbsp;5(d) are inclusive of any termination and/or severance payments

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; 
font-family:Times New Roman">(e) <U>Change of Control</U>. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:13%; font-size:10pt; 
font-family:Times New Roman">(i) Subject to Section&nbsp;5(e)(ii) below, within 
six (6)&nbsp;months following a Change of Control of the Company, should the 
Company not
renew or replace this Agreement with an Agreement containing substantially the 
same or better terms, the Executive shall be entitled to receive termination 
payments as set out in Section&nbsp;5(d) (but subject to the requirement of a 
full and final
release in favor of the Company in a form satisfactory to the Company), except 
that the 52-day period payment shall not apply, but instead the payment shall be
made as a single lump immediately following the expiration of a six 
(6)&nbsp;month period
from the date the Executive elected to terminate his employment with the 
Company. For the purposes of this Section&nbsp;5(e), &#147;Change of 
Control&#148; shall be defined as: (A)&nbsp;a tender offer or exchange offer is 
made and consummated for
the ownership of at least fifty percent (50%)&nbsp;of the outstanding voting 
securities of the Company; (B)&nbsp;the Company is merged or consolidated with 
another entity and as a result of such merger or consolidation, at least fifty 
percent
(50%)&nbsp;of the outstanding voting securities of the surviving or resulting 
entity is owned directly or indirectly in the aggregate by a person or persons 
other than a person or persons who owned at least fifty percent (50%)&nbsp;of 
the
outstanding voting securities of the Company immediately prior to such merger or
consolidation; (C)&nbsp;the Company is liquidated or otherwise sells or 
transfers all or substantially all of its assets to another entity which is not 
wholly owned,
directly or indirectly, by a person or persons who own at least fifty percent 
(50%)&nbsp;or more of the outstanding voting securities of the Company; or 
(D)&nbsp;a person, within the meaning of Section&nbsp;3(a)(9) or 
Section&nbsp;13(d)(3) of the
Securities Exchange Act of 1934, as amended and in effect from time to time, 
acquires over fifty percent (50%)&nbsp;or more of the outstanding voting 
securities of the Company (whether directly, indirectly, beneficially or of 
record). </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:13%; font-size:10pt; 
font-family:Times New Roman">(ii) Notwithstanding Section&nbsp;5(e)(i) hereof to

considered a Change of Control under this Section&nbsp;5(e) or under 
Section&nbsp;5(e) of
the Original Employment Agreement. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-

<U>Death</U>. The Executive&#146;s employment with the Company under this 
Agreement shall
automatically terminate upon the death of the Executive. Upon termination for 
death, the Executive or the Executive&#146;s estate shall only be entitled to

(ii)&nbsp;payment of any accrued but unused vacation pay; 
(iii)&nbsp;reimbursement of all out of pocket expenses in accordance with 
Section&nbsp;4(e); and (iv)&nbsp;notwithstanding any provision of any 
outstanding equity award agreements that might
otherwise be to the contrary, immediate acceleration of all unvested outstanding
equity awards under the Equity Incentive Plan or any equity incentive plan or 
long term incentive plan of the Company, such that all outstanding equity awards
which
have not already vested, shall immediately vest as of the Termination Date. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt;

the
Executive suffers a Permanent Disability (as defined below), the employment of 
the Executive may be terminated by the </P>

Company upon 90 days&#146; notice to the Executive; except that if the

vested, shall immediately vest as of the Termination Date. For the purposes of 
this Section&nbsp;5(g), &#147;Permanent Disability&#148; means a mental or 
physical disability whereby the Executive: </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:13%; font-size:10pt; 
font-family:Times New Roman">(i) is unable, due to illness, disease, mental or 
physical disability or similar cause, to fulfill his obligations as an employee 
or officer
of the Company either for three consecutive months or for a cumulative period of
6 months out of 12 consecutive calendar months, or </P> <P STYLE="margin-

New Roman">(ii)
is declared by a court of competent jurisdiction to be mentally incompetent or 
incapable of managing his affairs. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-

<U>Resignation as

together with any other office, position or directorship which the Executive may
hold with any of its affiliates. In such event, the Executive shall, at the

evidence such
resignations. The Executive shall not be entitled to any payments in respect of 
such resignations in addition to those provided for herein. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; 
font-family:Times New Roman">(i) <U>Survival</U>. Notwithstanding the 
termination of the Executive&#146;s employment, or the manner of termination, 
the provisions of
Sections 6 and 7 of this Agreement and the Non-Disclosure Agreement shall

Disclosure/Confidentiality
Obligations</U>. The parties contemplate the Executive providing executive

Executive&#146;s ability to perform these services, the Company agrees to

regarding the Company&#146;s business strategies, plans, techniques and 
processes, which are more
fully set forth in the Non-Disclosure Agreement (&#147;<U>Confidential 
Information</U>&#148;), which the Company uses to compete in the marketplace, 
and the Executive agrees not to use or disclose such Confidential Information 
for any purpose other
than to advance the Company&#146;s interests. Moreover, from time to time, 
subsidiary companies or affiliates of the Company may provide that entity&#146;s
confidential, proprietary information which

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times

the Company uses to compete in the marketplace, to the Executive to facilitate 
the Executive&#146;s ability to provide services to the subsidiary companies or 
affiliates, and the Executive agrees
not to use or disclose such Confidential Information for any purpose other than
to advance the subsidiary companies&#146; or affiliate&#146;s interests. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; 
font-family:Times New Roman">7. <U>Post-Employment Obligations</U>. During the 
Term of this Agreement and for twelve (12)&nbsp;months following the Termination
Date: </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; 
font-family:Times New Roman">(a) the Executive will not, as a competitor or on 
behalf of any competitor of the Company, directly or indirectly solicit or 
accept Business
from any Customer (as defined in the Non-Disclosure Agreement): (i)&nbsp;with 
whom the Executive had contact as a result of his duties with the Company or its
affiliates, and/or (ii)&nbsp;about whom the Executive reviewed or obtained 
Confidential
Information (as defined in the Non-Disclosure Agreement) while performing 
services for the Company or its affiliates. The geographic limitation for this 
restriction is (1)&nbsp;any Company or its affiliates&#146; territory in which 
the Executive had
a customer or service assignment for the Company or its affiliates in the twelve
(12)&nbsp;month period immediately preceding the Executive&#146;s Termination 
Date; and/or (2)&nbsp;any territory in which the Company or its affiliates, have
customers
or service assignments about which the Executive obtained Confidential 
Information during the term of this Agreement; and </P> <P STYLE="margin-
top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times 
New Roman">(b) the
Executive will not solicit, induce or attempt to induce any other employee, 
agent or contractor of the Company or its affiliates with whom the Executive 
worked or about whom the Executive obtained Confidential Information in the 
twelve
(12)&nbsp;month period immediately preceding the Executive&#146;s Termination 
Date, to leave the employ of the Company or its affiliates to work for a 
competitor of the Company or its affiliates in the same or similar capacity as 
the other employee,
agent or contractor of the Company or its affiliates worked for the Company or 
its affiliates. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-
indent:8%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(c) At the option of the
Company, and in
its sole discretion, the Company on the Termination Date may elect to extend the
provisions of Section&nbsp;7(a) and (b)&nbsp;for an additional twelve 
(12)&nbsp;months, in which case, the Company will pay to the Executive an amount
equal to twelve
(12)&nbsp;months of Base Salary as in effect at the Termination Date plus the 
Executive&#146;s annual performance cash award under Section&nbsp;4(c) hereof at
the Executive&#146;s Target Percentage of 100%, which shall be paid at the same 
time as
the lump sum cash payment is made pursuant to Section&nbsp;5(b), 5(d) or 5(e), 
as applicable, or, in the absence of such a payment, within 52 days following 
the Termination Date, in exchange for the Executive&#146;s continued compliance 
with the
provisions of Section&nbsp;7(a) and (b)&nbsp;for such additional twelve-month 
period. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-
size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">8. <U>Insurance.</U> </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; 
font-family:Times New Roman">(a) The Employer agrees to maintain throughout the 
term of this Agreement D&amp;O coverage substantially similar in nature to its 
current
D&amp;O coverage in effect immediately prior to the effective date of the RSA, 
providing coverage to the Executive for those claims and causes of action 
arising out the performance of the Executive&#146;s duties in the course and 
scope of his
employment under this Agreement. </P>

size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">10. <U>Specific Performance</U>. The 
Executive and
the Employer acknowledges that a remedy at law for any breach or threatened 
breach of Section&nbsp;6 or 7 of this Agreement will be inadequate and that each
Party may be entitled to specific performance, injunctive relief, and any other 
remedies
available to it for such breach or threatened breach. If a bond is required to 
be posted in order for either Party to secure an injunction, then the Parties 
stipulate that a bond in the amount of One Thousand and No/100 Dollars 
(US$1,000) will be
sufficient and reasonable in all circumstances to protect the rights of the 
Parties. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; 
font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">11. <U>Severability</U>. Whenever 
possible, each
provision of this Agreement shall be interpreted in such manner as to be 
effective and valid under applicable law, but if any provision of this Agreement
shall be prohibited by or invalid under applicable law, such provisions shall be
ineffective to
the extent of such provision or invalidity only, without invalidating the 
remainder of such provision or any remaining provisions of this Agreement. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; 
font-family:Times New Roman">12. <U>Assignment</U>. This Agreement may not be 
assigned by the Executive. Neither the Executive, his spouse, nor their estates 
shall have
any right to encumber or dispose of any right to receive payments under this 
Agreement, it being understood that such payments and the right thereto are 
nonassignable and nontransferable. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; 
font-family:Times New Roman">13. <U>Binding Effect</U>. Subject to the 
provisions of Section&nbsp;12 above, this Agreement shall be binding upon and 
inure to the benefit
of the Parties hereto, the Executive&#146;s heirs and personal representatives, 
and the successors and assignees of the Employer. </P> <P STYLE="margin-
top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times 
New Roman">14.
<U>Prior Employment Agreements and Obligations</U>. The Executive represents and
warrants to the Employer that he has fulfilled all of the terms and conditions 
of all prior </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P 
STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times 
New Roman">
employment agreements and employer policies to which he may be a party or have 
been a party, and that at the time of execution of this Agreement, the Executive
is not a party to or otherwise
restricted by any other employment agreement, non-solicitation agreement, non-
competition covenant, confidentiality or nondisclosure agreement (other than the
Non-Disclosure Agreement) in any manner which would prevent the Executive from 
performing
the services contemplated by this Agreement. The Executive represents and 
warrants that nothing contained in any agreement that he has with any parties 
shall preclude the Executive from performing all of his duties, obligations and 
covenants as
contained in this Agreement. The Employer is entering into this Agreement solely
for the expertise and experience of the Executive, and the Employer expressly 
forbids the Executive from using or disclosing any confidential information or 
trade
secrets of any prior employer or other third party in connection with the 
Executive&#146;s performance under this Agreement. The Executive represents and 
warrants to the Employer that he has not and will not in the future, take, use 
or disclose the
confidential information or trade secrets of a third-party for the benefit of 
the Employer. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%;
font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">15. <U>Parol Evidence</U>. This 
Agreement and
the Non-Disclosure Agreement (and any other agreements incorporated by reference
herein) constitutes the sole and complete agreement between the Parties hereto 
as to the matters contained herein, and no verbal or other statements, 
inducements or
representations have been made to or relied upon by either Party, and no 
modification hereof shall be effective unless in writing, signed, and executed 
in the same manner as this Agreement; <U>provided</U>, <U>however</U>, that the 
amount of
compensation to be paid to the Executive for services to be performed for the 
Employer may be changed from time to time by the Parties hereto by written 
agreement without in any other way modifying, changing, or affecting this 
Agreement and the
performance by the Executive of any of the duties of his employment with the 
Employer. The provisions of this Agreement supersede the provisions of the 
Original Employment Agreement in their entirety. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; 
font-family:Times New Roman">16. <U>Waiver</U>. Any waiver to be enforceable 
must be in writing and executed by the Party against whom the waiver is sought 
to be enforced.
</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-
size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">17. <U>Governing Law</U>. All issues and
questions concerning the construction, validity, enforcement and interpretation 
of this
Agreement shall be governed by, and construed in accordance with the State of 
Delaware, without giving effect to any choice of law or conflict of law rules or
provisions (whether of the state of Texas, Alaska, or any other jurisdiction) 
that would
cause the application of the laws of any jurisdiction other than the State of 
Delaware. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; 
font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">18. <U>Mutual Waiver of Jury 
Trial</U>. THE
EMPLOYER AND THE EXECUTIVE EACH WAIVE THEIR RESPECTIVE RIGHT TO A TRIAL BY JURY 
OF ANY CLAIM OR CAUSE OF ACTION BASED UPON OR ARISING OUT OR RELATED TO THIS 
AGREEMENT IN ANY ACTION, PROCEEDING OR OTHER LITIGATION OF ANY TYPE BROUGHT BY 
ANY OF THE
PARTIES AGAINST ANY OTHER PARTY OR ANY AFFILIATE OF ANY OTHER SUCH PARTY, 
WHETHER WITH RESPECT TO CONTRACT CLAIMS, TORT CLAIMS OR OTHERWISE. THE EMPLOYER 
AND THE EXECUTIVE EACH AGREE THAT ANY SUCH CLAIM OR CAUSE OF ACTION SHALL BE 
TRIED BY A COURT
TRIAL WITHOUT A JURY. WITHOUT LIMITING THE FOREGOING, THE PARTIES FURTHER AGREE 
THAT THEIR RESPECTIVE RIGHT TO A TRIAL BY JURY IS WAIVED BY OPERATION OF THIS 
SECTION AS TO ANY </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P 
STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New 
Roman" ALIGN="right">Amended and Restated
Executive Employment Agreement </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt;
font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="right">Page 12 </P>

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times 
New Roman">
ACTION, COUNTERCLAIM OR OTHER PROCEEDING WHICH SEEKS, IN WHOLE OR IN PART, TO 
CHALLENGE THE VALIDITY OR ENFORCEABILITY OF THIS AGREEMENT OR ANY PROVISION 
HEREOF. THIS WAIVER SHALL APPLY TO ANY
SUBSEQUENT AMENDMENTS, RENEWALS, SUPPLEMENTS OR MODIFICATIONS TO THIS AGREEMENT.
</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-
size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">19. <U>Attorneys&#146; Fees</U>. If any 
litigation is
instituted to enforce or interpret the provisions of this Agreement or the 
transactions described herein, the prevailing Party in such action shall be 
entitled to recover its reasonable attorneys&#146; fees from the other Party or 
Parties hereto.
</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-
size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">20. <U>Drafting</U>. Each of the Parties
hereto acknowledges that each Party was actively involved in the negotiation and
drafting of
this Agreement and that no law or rule of construction shall be raised or used 
in which the provisions of this Agreement shall be construed in favor or against
any Party hereto because one is deemed to be the author thereof. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; 
font-family:Times New Roman">21. <U>Multiple Counterparts</U>. This Agreement 
may be executed in multiple counterparts, including by facsimile transmission 
and email in
portable document format, each of which shall have the force and effect of an 
original, and all of which shall constitute one and the same agreement. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; 
font-family:Times New Roman">22. <U>Acknowledgment of Enforceability</U>. The 
Executive acknowledges and agrees that this Agreement contains reasonable 
limitations as to
time, geographical area, and scope of activity to be restrained that do not 
impose a greater restraint than is necessary to protect the goodwill or other 
business interest of the Employer. Therefore, the Executive agrees that all 
restrictions are
fairly compensated for and that no unreasonable restrictions exist. </P> <P 
STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-
family:Times New Roman">23. <U>Reconstruction of Agreement</U>. Should a court 
of competent
jurisdiction or an arbitrator having jurisdiction declare any of the provisions 
of this Agreement unenforceable due to any unreasonable restriction of time, 
geographical area, scope of activity, or otherwise, in lieu of declaring such 
provision
unenforceable, the court, to the extent permissible by law, shall, at the 
Employer&#146;s request, revise or reconstruct such provisions in a manner 
sufficient to cause them to be enforceable. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; 
font-family:Times New Roman">24. <U>Confidentiality</U>. The Executive 
acknowledges and agrees that the terms and conditions and the financial details 
of this Agreement
are confidential, and the Executive agrees that he will not disclose the same to
non-parties under any circumstances unless compelled by law. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; 
font-family:Times New Roman">25. <U>Section&nbsp;409A</U>. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; 
font-family:Times New Roman">(a) To the extent applicable, this Agreement shall 
be interpreted and administered in a manner so that any amount or benefit 
payable shall be
paid or provided in a manner that is either exempt from or compliant with the 
requirements of Section&nbsp;409A of the Internal Revenue Code of 1986, as 
amended, and applicable guidance and regulations issued thereunder 
(&#147;<U>Section
409A</U>&#148;). The parties agree to work together in good faith in an effort 
to comply with Section&nbsp;409A and any provision that would cause this 
Agreement to fail to satisfy Section&nbsp;409A shall have no force and effect 
until amended to
comply therewith (which </P>
<p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P 
STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New 
Roman" ALIGN="right">Amended and Restated
Executive Employment Agreement </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt;
font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="right">Page 13 </P>
<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times 
New Roman">
amendment may be retroactive to the extent permitted by Section&nbsp;409A). In 
addition, for purposes of this Agreement, each amount to be paid or benefit to 
be provided to the Executive pursuant
to this Agreement shall be construed as a separate identified payment for 
purposes of Section&nbsp;409A. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-
bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(b) 
With respect to any amount
of expenses eligible for reimbursement under this Agreement, such expenses shall
be reimbursed by the Company within thirty (30)&nbsp;days following the date on 
which the Company receives the applicable documentation from the Executive in 
accordance
with its expense reimbursement policies, but in no event later than the last day
of the Executive&#146;s taxable year following the taxable year in which the 
Executive incurs the related expenses. In no event shall the reimbursements or 
in-kind
benefits to be provided under this Agreement in one taxable year affect the 
amount of reimbursements or in-kind benefits to be provided in any other taxable
year, nor will the Executive&#146;s right to reimbursement or in-kind benefits 
be subject to
liquidation or exchange for another benefit. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; 
margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New 
Roman">(c) Notwithstanding any provision to the contrary in this Agreement, if 
the Executive is
deemed as of the Executive&#146;s Termination Date to be a &#147;Specified 
Employee&#148; within the meaning of that term under Code Section&nbsp;409A(a)
(2)(B), then with regard to any payment or the provision of any benefit that is 
required to be
delayed in compliance with Code Section&nbsp;409A(a)(2)(B), such payment or 
benefit (the &#147;Delayed Payment&#148;) shall not be made or provided prior to
the earlier of (i)&nbsp;the first business day of the seventh month measured 
from the date
of the Executive&#146;s separation from service (within the meaning of 
Section&nbsp;409A or (ii)&nbsp;the date of the Executive&#146;s death (the 
&#147;<U>Delay Period</U>&#148;). Upon the expiration of the Delay Period (the 
&#147;<U>Permissible
Payment Date</U>&#148;), all Delayed Payments (whether they would have otherwise
been payable in a single sum or in installments in the absence of such delay) 
shall be paid or reimbursed to the Executive in a lump sum on the Permissible 
Payment
Date, and any remaining payments and benefits due under this Agreement shall be 
paid or provided in accordance with the normal payment dates specified for them 
herein. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; 
font-family:Times New Roman">26. <U>Counsel</U>. The Executive acknowledges that
he is executing a legal document that contains certain duties, obligations and
restrictions as specified herein. The Executive furthermore acknowledges that he
has been advised of his right to retain legal counsel, and that he has either 
been represented by legal counsel prior to his execution hereof or has knowingly
elected
not to be so represented. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; 
text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">By signing below, 
the Executive acknowledges that he has received, read, and agrees to adhere to

conditions contained within this Agreement. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt;

 <BODY BGCOLOR="WHITE">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times 
New Roman" ALIGN="right"><B>Exhibit 10.2 </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times 
New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B><U>AMENDED AND RESTATED EXECUTIVE EMPLOYMENT 
AGREEMENT </U></B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; 
font-family:Times New Roman">THIS AMENDED AND RESTATED EXECUTIVE EMPLOYMENT 
AGREEMENT (the &#147;<U>Agreement</U>&#148;), effective as of the Effective Date
(as defined
below), is entered into by and between SAExploration Holdings, Inc., a Delaware 
corporation (the &#147;<U>Employer</U>&#148; or the &#147;<U>Company</U>&#148;),
and <U>Brian Beatty</U>, an individual residing in the Province of Alberta, 
Canada (the
&#147;<U>Executive</U>&#148;) and amends, restates and replaces in its entirety 
the Executive Employment Agreement dated as of June&nbsp;24, 2013, other than 
the provisions of the Non-Disclosure Agreement (as such term is defined herein) 
(the
&#147;<U>Original Employment Agreement</U>&#148;). The Employer and the 
Executive may be referred to singularly as &#147;<U>Party</U>&#148; or 
collectively as &#147;<U>Parties</U>.&#148; Unless otherwise specified, 
capitalized terms have the
meanings set forth herein. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:24pt; margin-bottom:0pt; 
font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><U>RECITALS </U></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; 
font-family:Times New Roman">WHEREAS, the Company and certain of its 
subsidiaries and such other parties identified therein entered into that certain
Restructuring Support
Agreement dated as of June&nbsp;13, 2016, whereby the parties thereto have 
agreed to enter into certain transactions that will have the effect of 
restructuring and recapitalizing the Company (the &#147;<U>RSA</U>&#148;) 
effective upon the Closing
Date (as such term is defined in the RSA); </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; 
margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New 
Roman">WHEREAS, prior to the Effective Date, the Employer has employed the 
Executive as Chief
Executive Officer and President; </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-
bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New 
Roman">WHEREAS, in connection with and pursuant to the provisions of the RSA, 
the Parties have agreed to amend
the Original Employment Agreement on the terms and conditions contained herein 
effective immediately upon the date of approval (the &#147;<U>Effective 
Date</U>&#148;) by the Board of Directors of the Company (the
&#147;<U>Board</U>&#148;); </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; 
font-family:Times New Roman">WHEREAS, effective immediately upon the Effective 
Date, the Company will employ the Executive as the Chief Operating Officer, and 
the
Executive desires to be employed by the Employer on the terms and conditions 
contained herein; </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-
indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">WHEREAS, the Employer 
acknowledges and
rewards the value and loyalty of the Executive and seeks to build and protect 
the Company&#146;s stability, growth, customer base, technology and other 
competitive advantages; and </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; 
font-family:Times New Roman">WHEREAS, the Executive wishes to evidence his 
commitment to the Company and its objectives. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; 
font-family:Times New Roman">NOW, THEREFORE, in consideration of the foregoing 
premises and the respective agreements hereinafter set forth and the mutual 
benefits to be
derived hereinafter, the Employer and the Executive hereby agree as follows: 
</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:24pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-
family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><U>AGREEMENTS </U></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; 
font-family:Times New Roman">1. <U>Employment Term</U>. The Employer hereby 
agrees to continue to employ the Executive commencing on the Effective Date and 
ending on the
third anniversary thereafter (the &#147;<U>Initial Term</U>&#148;); 
<U>provided</U>, <U>however</U>, that at the end of the Initial Term, the 
Executive&#146;s </P>
<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times 
New Roman">
employment and this Agreement shall automatically renew or extend for 
consecutive terms of one (1)&nbsp;year on each succeeding anniversary of the 
Effective Date (each such renewal or extension a
&#147;<U>Renewal Term</U>&#148;), unless either Party gives prior written notice
to the other Party of its desire to terminate the Agreement at least 90 days 
prior to the expiration of the Initial Term or any Renewal Term, as applicable 
(the Initial
Term and each Renewal Term, collectively, the &#147;<U>Term</U>&#148;). 
Notwithstanding the foregoing, the Parties shall have the termination rights as 
set forth in Section&nbsp;5 of this Agreement. Termination of this Agreement for
any reason
whatsoever by any Party shall have no effect on the continued enforceability of 
any ancillary agreement, specifically including the Non-Disclosure Agreement 
executed by the Executive in favor of the Employer concurrently with the 
Original Employment
Agreement, (the &#147;<U>Non-Disclosure Agreement</U>&#148;). The obligations of
the Parties under Sections 5 through 25 herein shall survive according to the 
terms of each provision. The Executive accepts such continued employment and 
agrees to
continue to perform the services specified herein, all upon the terms and 
conditions hereinafter stated. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-
bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">2. 
<U>Duties</U>. During the
Term, the Executive shall serve in the position of Chief Operating Officer and 
shall report to and be subject to the general direction and control of the Board
or its designee. In such capacity he shall be responsible for the supervision of
the day
to day operations of the Company and the implementation of its business plans 
and strategies, in each case, subject to the Board and in accordance with and 
subject to budgets approved from time to time by such Board. The Executive shall
perform such
duties consistent with the Executive&#146;s position, as well as other related 
duties from time to time assigned to the Executive by the Board. The Executive 
further agrees to perform, without additional compensation, such other services 
for the
Employer and for any of its affiliates as the Board shall from time to time 
specify, if such services are of the nature commonly associated with or similar 
to that of the Executive&#146;s position with a company engaged in activities 
similar to the
activities engaged in by the Employer at the time of execution of this 
Agreement. For purposes of the Non-Disclosure Agreement and Sections 5 through 
25 herein, the term &#147;Employer&#148; shall be deemed to include and refer to
any and all
affiliates of the Employer. The Executive acknowledges and agrees that the Non-
Disclosure Agreement executed simultaneously with the Original Employment 
Agreement is hereby incorporated by reference herein and made a part hereof and 
that the
Non-Disclosure Agreement constitutes a material part of this Agreement. </P> <P 
STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-
family:Times New Roman">3. <U>Extent of Service</U>. The Executive shall devote 
his full
business time, attention, and energy to the business of the Employer, and shall 
not be engaged in any other business activity that competes with or detracts 
from the business of the Employer during the Term of this Agreement. The 
foregoing shall not
be construed as preventing the Executive from making passive investments in 
other businesses or enterprises, if (i)&nbsp;such investments will not require 
services on the part of the Executive which would in any material way impair the
performance
of his duties under this Agreement, or (ii)&nbsp;such other businesses or 
enterprises are not engaged in any business competitive with the business of the
Employer or any of its affiliates. The Executive shall be based in the vicinity 
of the Calgary
metropolitan area (or such other area as may be agreed upon by the Parties) and,
subject to travel requirements as reasonably necessary to support successful 
business development efforts and management of the business, shall perform his 
services
from a mutually agreed location in that area. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P 
STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New 
Roman" ALIGN="right">Amended and Restated
Executive Employment Agreement </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt;
font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="right">Page 2 </P>
<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; 
font-family:Times New Roman">4. <U>Compensation and Benefits</U>. As payment for
the services to be rendered by the Executive
hereunder during the Term of this Agreement, the Executive shall be entitled to 
the following: </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-
indent:8%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(a) receive payment of 
the
Executive&#146;s annual base salary at the rate of not less than US$664,198.00 a
year (the &#147;<U>Base Salary</U>&#148;), less deductions required by law, 
payable in accordance with the Employer&#146;s standard payroll schedule, but 
not less
frequently than monthly; <U>provided</U>, that commencing with the 
Company&#146;s 2017 fiscal year, the Executive&#146;s Base Salary may be 
increased annually (but not decreased without the written consent of the 
Executive) in the discretion of the
Board; </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-
size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(b) a monthly automobile allowance of
US$2,750.00 per month payable in accordance with the Employer&#146;s standard 
payroll
schedule, and which shall be subject to customary deductions and withholding; 
</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-
size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(c) continue to be eligible to 
participate in any
short-term and long-term incentive compensation plans, annual bonus plans and 
such other management incentive programs or arrangements of the Company approved
by the Board that are generally available to the Company&#146;s senior 
executives and
continue to be eligible to receive annual performance cash awards 
(&#147;<U>Annual Cash Awards</U>&#148;) at the rate of 50% to 150% of Base 
Salary (the &#147;<U>Target Percentage</U>&#148;), and the Executive will be 
entitled to a guaranteed 50%
annual performance cash award and as much as 150% if certain executive goals 
(the &#147;Executive Goals&#148;) are reached as identified and approved by the 
Compensation Committee of the Board (the &#147;<U>Compensation 
Committee</U>&#148;), but not
to exceed the maximum award permissible under the applicable long-term incentive
plan for such annual award; <U>provided</U>, that, at the option of the 
Compensation Committee, up to 50% of any Annual Cash Award payable to the 
Executive may be paid
in shares of the Company&#146;s common stock (which is in addition to any shares
of the Company&#146;s common stock reserved for issuance under the SAExploration
Holdings, Inc. 2016 Long-Term Incentive Plan, as may be amended, restated and
supplemented from time to time (the &#147;<U>Equity Incentive Plan</U>&#148;)); 
<U>provided</U>, <U>further</U>, that such Target Percentage will be applied to 
twelve (12)&nbsp;times the highest paid monthly base salary within the 
applicable
calendar year. Commencing with the Company&#146;s 2017 fiscal year, the 
Executive Goals will be set by the Compensation Committee under the applicable 
long-term incentive plan for such annual award but in any event shall not exceed
the maximum award
permissible under such applicable plan; </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-
bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(d) the
Executive will be entitled to participate, on the same basis generally as other 
similarly
situated employees of the Company, in all benefits as may be offered by the 
Company from time to time; </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; 
text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(e) reimbursement 
of reasonable
expenses incurred by the Executive in accordance with such expense reimbursement
policies of the Company; and </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; 
text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(f) paid vacation 
of eight
(8)&nbsp;weeks per year. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; 
text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(g) <U>Equity 
Compensation</U>. The Executive shall be eligible to participate in the Equity 
Incentive Plan and
such other equity incentive programs or arrangements of the Company approved by 
the Board that are generally available to the Company&#146;s senior executives. 
The </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P

Board or the Compensation Committee, as applicable, pursuant to written
corporate action taken or at a meeting held, in either case, shall, effective on
September&nbsp;26, 2016 (the
&#147;<U>Grant Date</U>&#148;), subject to the Executive&#146;s employment on 
such Grant Date, award to the Executive the following: </P> <P STYLE="margin-

New Roman">(i)

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; 
font-family:Times New Roman"><U>provided</U>, <U>however</U>, that if the 
Executive&#146;s employment is terminated by reason
of the Executive&#146;s: (i)&nbsp;death; (ii)&nbsp;Permanent Disability; 
(iii)&nbsp;termination by the Company other than for Cause; or 
(iv)&nbsp;termination for Good Reason, all unvested portions of the 
Executive&#146;s MIP RSU Grant and the MIP
Option Grant shall become fully vested upon such termination. </P> <P 
STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:13%; font-size:10pt; 
font-family:Times New Roman">(iii) For the avoidance of doubt, the vesting of 
any awards granted to the
Executive under the Equity Incentive Plan shall not be conditioned on any 
financial, operating or other performance metrics. </P> <P STYLE="margin-
top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times 
New Roman">(h)
Notwithstanding any other provisions in this Agreement to the contrary, any 
incentive-based compensation, or any other compensation, paid to the Executive 
pursuant to this Agreement or any other agreement or arrangement with the 
Company which is
subject to recovery under any law, governmental regulation or stock exchange 
listing requirement or policy of the Company adopted to comply with any such 
law, regulation, or listing requirement, will be subject to such deductions and 
requirements
for repayment (&#147;<U>Clawback</U>&#148;) as may be required to be made 
pursuant to such law, governmental regulation, stock exchange listing 
requirement, or policy. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; 
font-family:Times New Roman">(i) Notwithstanding any provisions in this 
Agreement, the Equity Incentive Plan or any award agreement evidencing the 
grants set forth in
Section&nbsp;4(g) above to the contrary, if the Executive terminates his 
employment for any reason other than Good Reason prior to the first anniversary 
of the Closing Date, any awards granted pursuant to Section&nbsp;4(g) (whether
vested or
unvested) will be automatically forfeited, and the Executive will be required to
return and/or repay any shares or cash proceeds received in respect of such 
awards. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; 
font-family:Times New Roman">5. <U>Termination</U>. The Executive&#146;s 
employment with the Company under this Agreement may be terminated in accordance
with this
Section&nbsp;5. The date upon which any such termination becomes effective shall
be deemed the &#147;Termination Date&#148;. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; 
margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New 
Roman">(a)
<U>Termination by the Company for Cause</U>. The Company may terminate the 
Executive&#146;s employment with the Company under this Agreement for Cause at 
any time without notice and without any payment to the Executive whatsoever, 
save and except
for the payment of any Base Salary, vacation accrued but unpaid up to the 
Termination Date and out of pocket expenses in accordance with 
Section&nbsp;4(e), if the Executive engages in any of the following conduct 
(termination for
&#147;<U>Cause</U>&#148;): </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; 
text-indent:13%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(i) the breaching 
of any material provision of this Agreement after the Company has given the 
Executive not
less than 30 days written notice of such breach and a period of not less than 30
days to correct, or cause to be corrected, such breach; </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:13%; font-size:10pt; 
font-family:Times New Roman">(ii) knowing and intentional misappropriation of 
funds or property of the Company or its affiliates; </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:13%; font-size:10pt; 
font-family:Times New Roman">(iii) engaging in conduct, even if not in 
connection with the performance of the duties hereunder, which might be 
reasonably expected to
result in any effect materially adverse to the interests of the Company or any 
of its affiliates, such as fraud, dishonesty, conviction (or a judicial finding 
of evidence sufficient to convict) of any felony; </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P 
STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New 
Roman" ALIGN="right">Amended and Restated
Executive Employment Agreement </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt;
font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="right">Page 5 </P>
<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:13%; font-size:10pt; 
font-family:Times New Roman">(iv) failing to fulfill and perform the duties 
assigned to the Executive in accordance with the
terms herein after the Company has given the Executive not less than 15 days 
written notice of such failure and a period of not less than 15 days to correct,
or cause to be corrected, such failure; and </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:13%; font-size:10pt; 
font-family:Times New Roman">(v) failing to comply with corporate policies of 
the Company or any of its affiliates that are promulgated from time to time by 
the Company,
<U>provided</U>, <U>however</U>, that the Company shall not be unreasonably 
arbitrary in its enforcement of corporate policies with respect to the 
Executive. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; 
font-family:Times New Roman">(b) <U>Termination by the Executive for Good 
Reason</U>. The Executive shall have good reason (&#147;<U>Good 
Reason</U>&#148;) as defined
below to resign his employment within sixty (60)&nbsp;days following notice and 
receive the same payments as provided under Section&nbsp;5(d) (and subject to
the same release requirement), provided the Executive has first provided written
notice to
the Employer of conduct warranting termination of the Executive&#146;s 
employment for Good Reason and provided the Employer a period of not less than 
thirty (30)&nbsp;days to cure such conduct, without the written consent of the 
Executive: </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:13%; font-size:10pt; 
font-family:Times New Roman">(i) a material diminution in the nature and scope 
of the Executive&#146;s authorities or duties, including but not limited to a 
change in the
Executive&#146;s reporting relationship, a required move of more than a 50-mile 
radius of the Executive&#146;s employment prior to any such relocation, except 
for reasonably required travel on the Company&#146;s business or a reduction in 
pay (which
shall not be triggered by the Company&#146;s setting of the Executive Goals, 
beginning with the Company&#146;s 2017 fiscal year, pursuant Section&nbsp;4(c) 
above, even if the Executive&#146;s Annual Cash Award payout decreases as a 
result); or </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:13%; font-size:10pt; 
font-family:Times New Roman">(ii) a material breach of this Agreement by the 
Employer. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; 
font-family:Times New Roman">(c) <U>Termination by the Executive Without Good 
Reason</U>. The Executive may terminate his employment with the Company at any 
time, for any
reason, by providing 60 days&#146; advance written notice to the Company, which 
may be waived in whole or in part by the Company. If the Company waives the 
notice period in whole or in part, the Company shall pay the Base Salary for the
portion of
the notice period that has been waived. The Executive shall only be entitled to 
payment of any accrued but unpaid Base Salary, accrued but unpaid out of pocket 
expenses in accordance with Section&nbsp;4(e) hereof and vacation pay accrued 
but unpaid
up to the Termination Date. The Executive shall not be entitled to any accrued 
annual bonus or other benefits. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-
bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(d) 
<U>Termination by the
Company Without Cause</U>. The Company may terminate the Executive&#146;s 
employment, without Cause as defined in Sections 5(a), in which case the Company
shall pay the Executive the following, less withholdings required by law: </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:13%; font-size:10pt; 
font-family:Times New Roman">(i) all accrued but unpaid Base Salary to the 
Termination Date; </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:13%; font-size:10pt; 
font-family:Times New Roman">(ii) all accrued but unpaid vacation pay to the 
Termination Date; </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:13%; font-size:10pt; 
font-family:Times New Roman">(iii) payment equal to the previous two 
(2)&nbsp;years&#146; bonuses paid to the Executive, plus a prorated portion of 
any bonus for the year
of the Executive&#146;s termination in an </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P 
STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New 
Roman" ALIGN="right">Amended and Restated
Executive Employment Agreement </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt;
font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="right">Page 6 </P>

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times 
New Roman">
amount as provided under the applicable bonus plan of the Company, assuming a 
payment at the highest level of participation of the Target Percentage. If a
bonus payment was not paid to the
Executive in any of those previous two (2)&nbsp;years, this amount will be 
calculated on the assumption that the bonus paid for any unpaid year was paid in
full based upon the Executive&#146;s participation level in the applicable bonus
plan; </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:13%; font-size:10pt; 
font-family:Times New Roman">(iv) a severance amount equal to 24 months of Base 
Salary; </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:13%; font-size:10pt; 
font-family:Times New Roman">(v) if the Executive timely and properly elects 
continuation coverage under the Consolidated Omnibus Reconciliation Act of 1985
(&#147;<U>COBRA</U>&#148;), the Company shall reimburse the Executive for the 
monthly premiums associated with continuation of the Executive and his 
dependents&#146; insurance coverage. Such reimbursement shall be paid to the 
Executive on the 3rd
day of the month immediately following the month in which the Executive timely 
remits the premium payment (with the first such payment to be made on the first 
such date after the 52<SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">nd</SUP> 
day
following the Termination Date and shall include all amounts owed and due to be 
paid to the Executive but not paid due to such delay). The Executive shall be 
eligible to receive such reimbursement until the earliest of (x)&nbsp;the 18 
month
anniversary of the Termination Date; (y)&nbsp;the date the Executive is no 
longer eligible to receive COBRA continuation coverage; and (z)&nbsp;the date on
which the Executive becomes eligible to receive substantially similar coverage 
from another
employer; and </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-
indent:13%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(vi) notwithstanding 
any provision of any outstanding equity award agreement that might otherwise be 
to the contrary,
immediate acceleration of all unvested equity awards granted under the Equity 
Incentive Plan or any other equity incentive plan or long-term incentive plan of
the Company, such that all outstanding unvested equity awards which have not 
already
vested, shall immediately vest as of the Termination Date. </P> <P 
STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New
Roman">Prior to, and as a condition to, receiving the payments in this 
Section&nbsp;5(d) (other than
payments pursuant to Sections 5(d)(i) and (ii)), the Executive agrees to execute
a full and final release in favor of the Company, in a form satisfactory to the 
Company not later than fifty-two (52)&nbsp;days following the Termination Date. 
</P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; 
font-family:Times New Roman">The above amounts will be paid in a single lump sum
not later than fifty-two (52)&nbsp;days after the Termination Date subject to 
the
fulfillment of the provision of a full and final release no later than the end 
of such 52-day period; <U>provided</U> that the payments contemplated by 
Section&nbsp;5(d)(v) shall be reimbursed as set forth in Section&nbsp;5(d)(v). 
The above amounts
shall not be subject to the requirement of mitigation, nor reduced by any actual
mitigation by the Executive. The right to receive any of the above payments 
shall be forfeited if the required full and final release has not been received 
before the
end of the 52-day period; <U>provided</U>, <U>however</U>, if such 52-day period
begins in one taxable year and ends in a second taxable year, the payment date 
shall be deemed to be the later of (i)&nbsp;the first business day in the year 
following
the year in which the Executive&#146;s &#147;separation from service&#148; 
occurs or (ii)&nbsp;the last day of such 52-day period. The payments referred to
in Section&nbsp;5(d) are inclusive of any termination and/or severance payments 
that may be
required under applicable law. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-
bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(e) 
<U>Change of Control</U>. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P 
STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New

Executive Employment Agreement </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt;

<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
