 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:13%; font-size:10pt; 
font-family:Times New Roman">(i) Subject to Section&nbsp;5(e)(ii) below, within 
six (6)&nbsp;months following a Change of
Control of the Company, should the Company not renew or replace this Agreement 
with an Agreement containing substantially the same or better terms, the 
Executive shall be entitled to receive termination payments as set out in 
Section&nbsp;5(d) (but
subject to the requirement of a full and final release in favor of the Company 
in a form satisfactory to the Company), except that the 52-day period payment 
shall not apply, but instead the payment shall be made as a single lump 
immediately
following the expiration of a six (6)&nbsp;month period from the date the 
Executive elected to terminate his employment with the Company. For the purposes
of this Section&nbsp;5(e), &#147;Change of Control&#148; shall be defined as: 
(A)&nbsp;a
tender offer or exchange offer is made and consummated for the ownership of at 
least fifty percent (50%)&nbsp;of the outstanding voting securities of the 
Company; (B)&nbsp;the Company is merged or consolidated with another entity and 
as a result of
such merger or consolidation, at least fifty percent (50%)&nbsp;of the 
outstanding voting securities of the surviving or resulting entity is owned 
directly or indirectly in the aggregate by a person or persons other than a 
person or persons who
owned at least fifty percent (50%)&nbsp;of the outstanding voting securities of 
the Company immediately prior to such merger or consolidation; (C)&nbsp;the 
Company is liquidated or otherwise sells or transfers all or substantially all 
of its assets
to another entity which is not wholly owned, directly or indirectly, by a person
or persons who own at least fifty percent (50%)&nbsp;or more of the outstanding 
voting securities of the Company; or (D)&nbsp;a person, within the meaning of
Section&nbsp;3(a)(9) or Section&nbsp;13(d)(3) of the Securities Exchange Act of 
1934, as amended and in effect from time to time, acquires over fifty percent 
(50%)&nbsp;or more of the outstanding voting securities of the Company (whether 
directly,
indirectly, beneficially or of record). </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-
bottom:0pt; text-indent:13%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(ii) 
Notwithstanding Section&nbsp;5(e)(i) hereof to the contrary, the Executive 
acknowledges and
agrees that the Executive has waived such provision and the corresponding 
provision under Section&nbsp;5(e) of the Original Employment Agreement and any 
right to claim any such compensation and benefits provided under this Agreement 
in connection
therewith with respect to the transactions specified in the RSA (the 
&#147;<U>Restructuring Transactions</U>&#148;), and further acknowledges and 
agrees that the Restructuring Transactions shall not be considered a Change of 
Control under this
Section&nbsp;5(e) or under Section&nbsp;5(e) of the Original Employment 
Agreement. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; 
font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(f) <U>Death</U>. The 
Executive&#146;s employment with
the Company under this Agreement shall automatically terminate upon the death of
the Executive. Upon termination for death, the Executive or the Executive&#146;s
estate shall only be entitled to (i)&nbsp;payment of any portion of the Base
Salary due
and owing up to such date; (ii)&nbsp;payment of any accrued but unused vacation 
pay; (iii)&nbsp;reimbursement of all out of pocket expenses in accordance with 
Section&nbsp;4(e); and (iv)&nbsp;notwithstanding any provision of any 
outstanding equity
award agreements that might otherwise be to the contrary, immediate acceleration
of all unvested outstanding equity awards under the Equity Incentive Plan or any
equity incentive plan or long term incentive plan of the Company, such that all
outstanding equity awards which have not already vested, shall immediately vest 
as of the Termination Date. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; 
text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(g) <U>Permanent
Disability</U>. In the event that the Executive suffers a Permanent Disability 
(as defined below), the employment of the Executive may be terminated by the 
Company upon 90 days&#146; notice to the Executive; except that if the 
termination of the
Executive&#146;s employment would impair his ability to receive long term 
disability benefits in whole or in part, </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P 
STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New 
Roman" ALIGN="right">Amended and Restated
Executive Employment Agreement </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt;

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times 
New Roman">
the Executive shall, in lieu of termination, be placed on an unpaid leave of 
absence, it being understood, however, that the Executive shall not be entitled 
to re-employment by the Company after
such leave of absence or when he ceases to be in receipt of such benefits. Upon 
termination of employment for Permanent Disability, the Executive or the 
Executive&#146;s estate shall only be entitled to (i)&nbsp;payment of any 
portion of the Base
Salary due and owing up to such date; (ii)&nbsp;reimbursement of all expenses in
accordance with Section&nbsp;4(e); (iii)&nbsp;payment for any accrued but unused
vacation pay; and (iv)&nbsp;notwithstanding any provision of any outstanding 
equity
award agreements that might otherwise be to the contrary, immediate acceleration
of all unvested outstanding equity awards under the Equity Incentive Plan or any
equity incentive plan or long term incentive plan of the Company, such that all
outstanding equity awards which have not already vested, shall immediately vest 
as of the Termination Date. For the purposes of this Section&nbsp;5(g), 
&#147;Permanent Disability&#148; means a mental or physical disability whereby 
the Executive:
</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:13%; font-
size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(i) is unable, due to illness, disease, 
mental or physical disability or similar cause, to fulfill his obligations as an
employee or
officer of the Company either for three consecutive months or for a cumulative 
period of 6 months out of 12 consecutive calendar months, or </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:13%; font-size:10pt; 
font-family:Times New Roman">(ii) is declared by a court of competent 
jurisdiction to be mentally incompetent or incapable of managing his affairs. 
</P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; 
font-family:Times New Roman">(h) <U>Resignation as Officer or Director Upon 
Termination</U>. Upon termination of his employment for any reason whatsoever, 
the Executive
shall thereupon be deemed to have immediately resigned any position the 
Executive may have as an officer or director of the Company together with any 
other office, position or directorship which the Executive may hold with any of 
its affiliates. In
such event, the Executive shall, at the request of the Company, forthwith 
execute any and all documents appropriate to evidence such resignations. The 
Executive shall not be entitled to any payments in respect of such resignations 
in addition to
those provided for herein. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; 
text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(i) 
<U>Survival</U>. Notwithstanding the termination of the Executive&#146;s 
employment, or the manner of
termination, the provisions of Sections 6 and 7 of this Agreement and the Non-
Disclosure Agreement shall survive such termination. </P> <P STYLE="margin-
top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times 
New Roman">6.
<U>Non-Disclosure/Confidentiality Obligations</U>. The parties contemplate the 
Executive providing executive services to the Company in connection with its 
core business of providing effective acquisition of seismic data (the
&#147;<U>Business</U>&#148;). To facilitate the Executive&#146;s ability to 
perform these services, the Company agrees to provide the Executive 
confidential, proprietary, trade secret information regarding the Company&#146;s
business strategies,
plans, techniques and processes, which are more fully set forth in the Non-
Disclosure Agreement (&#147;<U>Confidential Information</U>&#148;), which the 
Company uses to compete in the marketplace, and the Executive agrees not to use 
or disclose such
Confidential Information for any purpose other than to advance the 
Company&#146;s interests. Moreover, from time to time, subsidiary companies or 
affiliates of the Company may provide that entity&#146;s confidential, 
proprietary information which
the Company uses to compete in the marketplace, to the Executive to facilitate 
the Executive&#146;s ability to provide services to the subsidiary companies or 
affiliates, and the Executive agrees not to use or disclose such Confidential 
Information
for any purpose other than to advance the subsidiary companies&#146; or 
affiliate&#146;s interests. </P>

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; 
font-family:Times New Roman">7. <U>Post-Employment Obligations</U>. During the 
Term of this Agreement and for twelve
(12)&nbsp;months following the Termination Date: </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt;
margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New 
Roman">(a) the Executive will not, as a competitor or on behalf of any 
competitor of the
Company, directly or indirectly solicit or accept Business from any Customer (as
defined in the Non-Disclosure Agreement): (i)&nbsp;with whom the Executive had 
contact as a result of his duties with the Company or its affiliates, and/or
(ii)&nbsp;about whom the Executive reviewed or obtained Confidential Information
(as defined in the Non-Disclosure Agreement) while performing services for the 
Company or its affiliates. The geographic limitation for this restriction is 
(1)&nbsp;any
Company or its affiliates&#146; territory in which the Executive had a customer 
or service assignment for the Company or its affiliates in the twelve 
(12)&nbsp;month period immediately preceding the Executive&#146;s Termination 
Date; and/or
(2)&nbsp;any territory in which the Company or its affiliates, have customers or
service assignments about which the Executive obtained Confidential Information 
during the term of this Agreement; and </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt;
font-family:Times New Roman">(b) the Executive will not solicit, induce or 
attempt to induce any other employee, agent or contractor of the Company or its 
affiliates with
whom the Executive worked or about whom the Executive obtained Confidential 
Information in the twelve (12)&nbsp;month period immediately preceding the 
Executive&#146;s Termination Date, to leave the employ of the Company or its 
affiliates to work
for a competitor of the Company or its affiliates in the same or similar 
capacity as the other employee, agent or contractor of the Company or its 
affiliates worked for the Company or its affiliates. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; 
font-family:Times New Roman">(c) At the option of the Company, and in its sole 
discretion, the Company on the Termination Date may elect to extend the 
provisions of
Section&nbsp;7(a) and (b)&nbsp;for an additional twelve (12)&nbsp;months, in 
which case, the Company will pay to the Executive an amount equal to twelve 
(12)&nbsp;months of Base Salary as in effect at the Termination Date plus the 
Executive&#146;s
annual performance cash award under Section&nbsp;4(c) hereof at the 
Executive&#146;s Target Percentage of 100%, which shall be paid at the same time
as the lump sum cash payment is made pursuant to Section&nbsp;5(b), 5(d) or 
5(e), as applicable, or,
in the absence of such a payment, within 52 days following the Termination Date,
in exchange for the Executive&#146;s continued compliance with the provisions of
Section&nbsp;7(a) and (b)&nbsp;for such additional twelve-month period. </P>

ineffective to

assigned by the Executive. Neither the Executive, his spouse, nor their estates 
shall have
any right to encumber or dispose of any right to receive payments under this 
Agreement, it being understood that such payments and the right thereto are 
nonassignable and nontransferable. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; 
font-family:Times New Roman">13. <U>Binding Effect</U>. Subject to the 
provisions of Section&nbsp;12 above, this Agreement shall be binding upon and 
inure to the benefit
of the Parties hereto, the Executive&#146;s heirs and personal representatives, 
and the successors and assignees of the Employer. </P> <P STYLE="margin-
top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times 
New Roman">14.
<U>Prior Employment Agreements and Obligations</U>. The Executive represents and
warrants to the Employer that he has fulfilled all of the terms and conditions 
of all prior employment agreements and employer policies to which he may be a 
party or
have been a party, and that at the time of execution of this Agreement, the 
Executive is not a party to or otherwise restricted by any other employment 
agreement, non-solicitation agreement, non-competition covenant, confidentiality
or nondisclosure
agreement (other than the Non-Disclosure Agreement) </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P 
STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New 
Roman" ALIGN="right">Amended and Restated
Executive Employment Agreement </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt;
font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="right">Page 11 </P>
<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times 
New Roman">
in any manner which would prevent the Executive from performing the services 
contemplated by this Agreement. The Executive represents and warrants that 
nothing contained in any agreement that he
has with any parties shall preclude the Executive from performing all of his 
duties, obligations and covenants as contained in this Agreement. The Employer 
is entering into this Agreement solely for the expertise and experience of the 
Executive, and
the Employer expressly forbids the Executive from using or disclosing any 
confidential information or trade secrets of any prior employer or other third 
party in connection with the Executive&#146;s performance under this Agreement. 
The Executive
represents and warrants to the Employer that he has not and will not in the 
future, take, use or disclose the confidential information or trade secrets of a
third-party for the benefit of the Employer. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; 
font-family:Times New Roman">15. <U>Parol Evidence</U>. This Agreement and the 
Non-Disclosure Agreement (and any other agreements incorporated by reference 
herein)
constitutes the sole and complete agreement between the Parties hereto as to the
matters contained herein, and no verbal or other statements, inducements or 
representations have been made to or relied upon by either Party, and no 
modification hereof
shall be effective unless in writing, signed, and executed in the same manner as
this Agreement; <U>provided</U>, <U>however</U>, that the amount of compensation
to be paid to the Executive for services to be performed for the Employer may be
changed from time to time by the Parties hereto by written agreement without in 
any other way modifying, changing, or affecting this Agreement and the 
performance by the Executive of any of the duties of his employment with the 
Employer. The
provisions of this Agreement supersede the provisions of the Original Employment
Agreement in their entirety. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; 
text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">16. <U>Waiver</U>. 
Any
waiver to be enforceable must be in writing and executed by the Party against 
whom the waiver is sought to be enforced. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; 
margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New 
Roman">17. <U>Governing
Law</U>. All issues and questions concerning the construction, validity, 
enforcement and interpretation of this Agreement shall be governed by, and 
construed in accordance with the State of Delaware, without giving effect to any
choice of law or
conflict of law rules or provisions (whether of the state of Texas, Alaska, or 
any other jurisdiction) that would cause the application of the laws of any 
jurisdiction other than the State of Delaware. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; 
font-family:Times New Roman">18. <U>Mutual Waiver of Jury Trial</U>. THE 
EMPLOYER AND THE EXECUTIVE EACH WAIVE THEIR RESPECTIVE RIGHT TO A TRIAL BY JURY 
OF ANY CLAIM OR
CAUSE OF ACTION BASED UPON OR ARISING OUT OR RELATED TO THIS AGREEMENT IN ANY 
ACTION, PROCEEDING OR OTHER LITIGATION OF ANY TYPE BROUGHT BY ANY OF THE PARTIES
AGAINST ANY OTHER PARTY OR ANY AFFILIATE OF ANY OTHER SUCH PARTY, WHETHER WITH 
RESPECT TO
CONTRACT CLAIMS, TORT CLAIMS OR OTHERWISE. THE EMPLOYER AND THE EXECUTIVE EACH 
AGREE THAT ANY SUCH CLAIM OR CAUSE OF ACTION SHALL BE TRIED BY A COURT TRIAL 
WITHOUT A JURY. WITHOUT LIMITING THE FOREGOING, THE PARTIES FURTHER AGREE THAT 
THEIR
RESPECTIVE RIGHT TO A TRIAL BY JURY IS WAIVED BY OPERATION OF THIS SECTION AS TO
ANY ACTION, COUNTERCLAIM OR OTHER PROCEEDING WHICH SEEKS, IN WHOLE OR IN PART, 
TO CHALLENGE THE VALIDITY OR ENFORCEABILITY OF THIS AGREEMENT OR ANY PROVISION 
HEREOF.
THIS WAIVER SHALL APPLY TO ANY SUBSEQUENT AMENDMENTS, RENEWALS, SUPPLEMENTS OR 
MODIFICATIONS TO THIS AGREEMENT. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P 
STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New 
Roman" ALIGN="right">Amended and Restated
Executive Employment Agreement </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt;

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt;

is instituted to enforce or interpret the
provisions of this Agreement or the transactions described herein, the 
prevailing Party in such action shall be entitled to recover its reasonable 
attorneys&#146; fees from the other Party or Parties hereto. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; 
font-family:Times New Roman">20. <U>Drafting</U>. Each of the Parties hereto 
acknowledges that each Party was actively involved in the negotiation and 
drafting of this
Agreement and that no law or rule of construction shall be raised or used in 
which the provisions of this Agreement shall be construed in favor or against 
any Party hereto because one is deemed to be the author thereof. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; 
font-family:Times New Roman">21. <U>Multiple Counterparts</U>. This Agreement 
may be executed in multiple counterparts, including by facsimile transmission 
and email in
portable document format, each of which shall have the force and effect of an 
original, and all of which shall constitute one and the same agreement. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; 
font-family:Times New Roman">22. <U>Acknowledgment of Enforceability</U>. The 
Executive acknowledges and agrees that this Agreement contains reasonable 
limitations as to
time, geographical area, and scope of activity to be restrained that do not 
impose a greater restraint than is necessary to protect the goodwill or other 
business interest of the Employer. Therefore, the Executive agrees that all 
restrictions are
fairly compensated for and that no unreasonable restrictions exist. </P> <P 
STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-
family:Times New Roman">23. <U>Reconstruction of Agreement</U>. Should a court 
of competent
jurisdiction or an arbitrator having jurisdiction declare any of the provisions 
of this Agreement unenforceable due to any unreasonable restriction of time, 
geographical area, scope of activity, or otherwise, in lieu of declaring such 
provision
unenforceable, the court, to the extent permissible by law, shall, at the 
Employer&#146;s request, revise or reconstruct such provisions in a manner 
sufficient to cause them to be enforceable. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; 
font-family:Times New Roman">24. <U>Confidentiality</U>. The Executive 
acknowledges and agrees that the terms and conditions and the financial details 
of this Agreement
are confidential, and the Executive agrees that he will not disclose the same to
non-parties under any circumstances unless compelled by law. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; 
font-family:Times New Roman">25. <U>Section&nbsp;409A</U>. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; 
font-family:Times New Roman">(a) To the extent applicable, this Agreement shall 
be interpreted and administered in a manner so that any amount or benefit 
payable shall be
paid or provided in a manner that is either exempt from or compliant with the 
requirements of Section&nbsp;409A of the Internal Revenue Code of 1986, as 
amended, and applicable guidance and regulations issued thereunder 
(&#147;<U>Section
409A</U>&#148;). The parties agree to work together in good faith in an effort 
to comply with Section&nbsp;409A and any provision that would cause this 
Agreement to fail to satisfy Section&nbsp;409A shall have no force and effect 
until amended to
comply therewith (which amendment may be retroactive to the extent permitted by 
Section&nbsp;409A). In addition, for purposes of this Agreement, each amount to 
be paid or benefit to be provided to the Executive pursuant to this Agreement 
shall be
construed as a separate identified payment for purposes of Section&nbsp;409A. 
</P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P 
STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New 
Roman" ALIGN="right">Amended and Restated
Executive Employment Agreement </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt;

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; 
font-family:Times New Roman">(b) With respect to any amount of expenses eligible
for reimbursement under this Agreement, such
expenses shall be reimbursed by the Company within thirty (30)&nbsp;days 
following the date on which the Company receives the applicable documentation 
from the Executive in accordance with its expense reimbursement policies, but in
no event later
than the last day of the Executive&#146;s taxable year following the taxable 
year in which the Executive incurs the related expenses. In no event shall the 
reimbursements or in-kind benefits to be provided under this Agreement in one 
taxable year
affect the amount of reimbursements or in-kind benefits to be provided in any 
other taxable year, nor will the Executive&#146;s right to reimbursement or in-
kind benefits be subject to liquidation or exchange for another benefit. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; 
font-family:Times New Roman">(c) Notwithstanding any provision to the contrary 
in this Agreement, if the Executive is deemed as of the Executive&#146;s 
Termination Date to
be a &#147;Specified Employee&#148; within the meaning of that term under Code 
Section&nbsp;409A(a)(2)(B), then with regard to any payment or the provision of 
any benefit that is required to be delayed in compliance with Code
Section&nbsp;409A(a)(2)(B), such payment or benefit (the &#147;Delayed 
Payment&#148;) shall not be made or provided prior to the earlier of 
(i)&nbsp;the first business day of the seventh month measured from the date of 
the Executive&#146;s
separation from service (within the meaning of Section&nbsp;409A or 
(ii)&nbsp;the date of the Executive&#146;s death (the &#147;<U>Delay 
Period</U>&#148;). Upon the expiration of the Delay Period (the 
&#147;<U>Permissible Payment Date</U>&#148;),
all Delayed Payments (whether they would have otherwise been payable in a single
sum or in installments in the absence of such delay) shall be paid or reimbursed
to the Executive in a lump sum on the Permissible Payment Date, and any 
remaining
payments and benefits due under this Agreement shall be paid or provided in 
accordance with the normal payment dates specified for them herein. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; 
font-family:Times New Roman">26. <U>Counsel</U>. The Executive acknowledges that
he is executing a legal document that contains certain duties, obligations and

has been advised of his right to retain legal counsel, and that he has either 
been represented by legal counsel prior to his execution hereof or has knowingly
elected
not to be so represented. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt;

the Executive acknowledges that he has received, read, and agrees to adhere to

conditions contained within this Agreement. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt;

 <BODY BGCOLOR="WHITE">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times 
New Roman" ALIGN="right"><B>Exhibit 10.3 </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times 
New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B><U>AMENDED AND RESTATED EXECUTIVE EMPLOYMENT 
AGREEMENT </U></B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; 
font-family:Times New Roman">THIS AMENDED AND RESTATED EXECUTIVE EMPLOYMENT 
AGREEMENT (the &#147;<U>Agreement</U>&#148;), effective as of the Effective Date
(as defined
below), is entered into by and between SAExploration Holdings, Inc., a Delaware
corporation (the &#147;<U>Employer</U>&#148; or the &#147;<U>Company</U>&#148;),
and <U>Brent Whiteley</U>, an individual residing in Houston, Texas (the
&#147;<U>Executive</U>&#148;) and amends, restates and replaces in its entirety 
the Executive Employment Agreement dated as of June&nbsp;24, 2013, other than 
the provisions of the Non-Disclosure Agreement (as such term is defined herein) 
(the
&#147;<U>Original Employment Agreement</U>&#148;). The Employer and the 
Executive may be referred to singularly as &#147;<U>Party</U>&#148; or 
collectively as &#147;<U>Parties</U>.&#148; Unless otherwise specified, 
capitalized terms have the
meanings set forth herein. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:24pt; margin-bottom:0pt; 
font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><U>RECITALS </U></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; 
font-family:Times New Roman">WHEREAS, the Company and certain of its 
subsidiaries and such other parties identified therein entered into that certain
Restructuring Support
Agreement dated as of June&nbsp;13, 2016, whereby the parties thereto have 
agreed to enter into certain transactions that will have the effect of 
restructuring and recapitalizing the Company (the &#147;<U>RSA</U>&#148;) 
effective upon the Closing
Date (as such term is defined in the RSA); </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; 
margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New 
Roman">WHEREAS, prior to the Effective Date, the Employer has employed the 
Executive as Chief
Financial Officer, General Counsel and Secretary; </P> <P STYLE="margin-
top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times 
New Roman">WHEREAS, in connection with and pursuant to the provisions of the 
RSA, the Parties have
agreed to amend the Original Employment Agreement on the terms and conditions 
contained herein effective immediately upon the date of approval (the 
&#147;<U>Effective Date</U>&#148;) by the Board of Directors of the Company (the
&#147;<U>Board</U>&#148;); </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; 
text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">WHEREAS, effective 
immediately upon the Effective Date, the Company will continue to employ the 
Executive as
the Chief Financial Officer, General Counsel and Secretary, and the Executive 
desires to be employed by the Employer on the terms and conditions contained 
herein; </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; 
font-family:Times New Roman">WHEREAS, the Employer acknowledges and rewards the 
value and loyalty of the Executive and seeks to build and protect the 
Company&#146;s
stability, growth, customer base, technology and other competitive advantages; 
and </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-
size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">WHEREAS, the Executive wishes to 
evidence his
commitment to the Company and its objectives. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; 
margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New 
Roman">NOW, THEREFORE, in consideration of the foregoing premises and the 
respective agreements
hereinafter set forth and the mutual benefits to be derived hereinafter, the 
Employer and the Executive hereby agree as follows: </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:24pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times 
New Roman" ALIGN="center"><U>AGREEMENTS </U></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; 
margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New 
Roman">1.
<U>Employment Term</U>. The Employer hereby agrees to continue to employ the 
Executive commencing on the Effective Date and ending on the third anniversary 
thereafter (the &#147;<U>Initial Term</U>&#148;); <U>provided</U>, 
<U>however</U>, that at
the end of the Initial Term, the Executive&#146;s </P>
<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times 
New Roman">
employment and this Agreement shall automatically renew or extend for 
consecutive terms of one (1)&nbsp;year on each succeeding anniversary of the 
Effective Date (each such renewal or extension a
&#147;<U>Renewal Term</U>&#148;), unless either Party gives prior written notice
to the other Party of its desire to terminate the Agreement at least 90 days 
prior to the expiration of the Initial Term or any Renewal Term, as applicable 
(the Initial
Term and each Renewal Term, collectively, the &#147;<U>Term</U>&#148;). 
Notwithstanding the foregoing, the Parties shall have the termination rights as 
set forth in Section&nbsp;5 of this Agreement. Termination of this Agreement for
any reason
whatsoever by any Party shall have no effect on the continued enforceability of 
any ancillary agreement, specifically including the Non-Disclosure Agreement 
executed by the Executive in favor of the Employer concurrently with the 
Original Employment
Agreement, (the &#147;<U>Non-Disclosure Agreement</U>&#148;). The obligations of
the Parties under Sections 5 through 25 herein shall survive according to the 
terms of each provision. The Executive accepts such continued employment and 
agrees to
continue to perform the services specified herein, all upon the terms and 
conditions hereinafter stated. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-
bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">2. 
<U>Duties</U>. During the
Term, the Executive shall serve in the position of Chief Financial Officer, 
General Counsel and Secretary and shall report to and be subject to the general 
direction and control of the Board or its designee. In such capacity he shall be
responsible
for the supervision of the day to day operations of the Company and the 
implementation of its business plans and strategies, in each case, subject to 
the Board and in accordance with and subject to budgets approved from time to 
time by such Board.
The Executive shall perform such duties consistent with the Executive&#146;s 
position, as well as other related duties from time to time assigned to the 
Executive by the Board. The Executive further agrees to perform, without 
additional
compensation, such other services for the Employer and for any of its affiliates
as the Board shall from time to time specify, if such services are of the nature
commonly associated with or similar to that of the Executive&#146;s position 
with a
company engaged in activities similar to the activities engaged in by the 
Employer at the time of execution of this Agreement. For purposes of the Non-
Disclosure Agreement and Sections 5 through 25 herein, the term 
&#147;Employer&#148; shall be
deemed to include and refer to any and all affiliates of the Employer. The 
Executive acknowledges and agrees that the Non-Disclosure Agreement executed 
simultaneously with the Original Employment Agreement is hereby incorporated by 
reference herein
and made a part hereof and that the Non-Disclosure Agreement constitutes a 
material part of this Agreement. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-
bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">3. 
<U>Extent of Service</U>.
The Executive shall devote his full business time, attention, and energy to the 
business of the Employer, and shall not be engaged in any other business 
activity that competes with or detracts from the business of the Employer during
the Term of
this Agreement. The foregoing shall not be construed as preventing the Executive
from making passive investments in other businesses or enterprises, if 
(i)&nbsp;such investments will not require services on the part of the Executive
which would in
any material way impair the performance of his duties under this Agreement, or 
(ii)&nbsp;such other businesses or enterprises are not engaged in any business 
competitive with the business of the Employer or any of its affiliates. The
Executive shall
be based in the vicinity of the Houston metropolitan area (or such other area as
may be agreed upon by the Parties) and, subject to travel requirements as 
reasonably necessary to support successful business development efforts and 
management of the
business, shall perform his services from a mutually agreed location in that 
area. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P 
STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New 
Roman" ALIGN="right">Amended and Restated
Executive Employment Agreement </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt;
font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="right">Page 2 </P>
<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; 
font-family:Times New Roman">4. <U>Compensation and Benefits</U>. As payment for
the services to be rendered by the Executive
hereunder during the Term of this Agreement, the Executive shall be entitled to 
the following: </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-
indent:8%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(a) receive payment of 
the
Executive&#146;s annual base salary at the rate of not less than US$448,231.00 a
year (the &#147;<U>Base Salary</U>&#148;), less deductions required by law, 
payable in accordance with the Employer&#146;s standard payroll schedule, but 
not less
frequently than monthly; <U>provided</U>, that commencing with the 
Company&#146;s 2017 fiscal year, the Executive&#146;s Base Salary may be 
increased annually (but not decreased without the written consent of the 
Executive) in the discretion of the
Board; </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-
size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(b) a monthly automobile allowance of 
US$1,750.00 per month payable in accordance with the Employer&#146;s standard 
payroll
schedule, and which shall be subject to customary deductions and withholding; 
</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-
size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(c) continue to be eligible to 
participate in any
short-term and long-term incentive compensation plans, annual bonus plans and 
such other management incentive programs or arrangements of the Company approved
by the Board that are generally available to the Company&#146;s senior 
executives and
continue to be eligible to receive annual performance cash awards 
(&#147;<U>Annual Cash Awards</U>&#148;) at the rate of 40% to 120% of Base 
Salary (the &#147;<U>Target Percentage</U>&#148;), and the Executive will be 
entitled to a guaranteed 40%
annual performance cash award and as much as 120% if certain executive goals 
(the &#147;<U>Executive Goals</U>&#148;) are reached as identified and approved 
by the Compensation Committee of the Board (the &#147;<U>Compensation 
Committee</U>&#148;),
but not to exceed the maximum award permissible under the applicable long-term 
incentive plan for such annual award; <U>provided</U>, that, at the option of 
the Compensation Committee, up to 50% of any Annual Cash Award payable to the 
Executive may
be paid in shares of the Company&#146;s common stock (which is in addition to 
any shares of the Company&#146;s common stock reserved for issuance under the 
SAExploration Holdings, Inc. 2016 Long-Term Incentive Plan, as may be amended, 
restated and
supplemented from time to time (the &#147;<U>Equity Incentive Plan</U>&#148;)); 
<U>provided</U>, <U>further</U>, that such Target Percentage will be applied to 
twelve (12)&nbsp;times the highest paid monthly base salary within the 
applicable
calendar year. Commencing with the Company&#146;s 2017 fiscal year, the
Executive Goals will be set by the Compensation Committee under the applicable 
long-term incentive plan for such annual award but in any event shall not exceed
the maximum award
permissible under such applicable plan; </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-
bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(d) the
Executive will be entitled to participate, on the same basis generally as other 
similarly
situated employees of the Company, in all benefits as may be offered by the 
Company from time to time; </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; 
text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(e) reimbursement 
of reasonable
expenses incurred by the Executive in accordance with such expense reimbursement
policies of the Company; and </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; 
text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(f) paid vacation 
of six
(6)&nbsp;weeks per year. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; 
text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(g) <U>Equity 
Compensation</U>. The Executive shall be eligible to participate in the Equity 
Incentive Plan and
such other equity incentive programs or arrangements of the Company approved by 
the Board that are generally available to the Company&#146;s senior executives.

<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; 
font-family:Times New Roman">5. <U>Termination</U>. The Executive&#146;s 
employment with the Company under this Agreement may be terminated in accordance
with this
Section&nbsp;5. The date upon which any such termination becomes effective shall
be deemed the &#147;Termination Date&#148;. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; 
margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New 
Roman">(a)
<U>Termination by the Company for Cause</U>. The Company may terminate the 
Executive&#146;s employment with the Company under this Agreement for Cause at 
any time without notice and without any payment to the Executive whatsoever, 
save and except
for the payment of any Base Salary, vacation accrued but unpaid up to the 
Termination Date and out of pocket expenses in accordance with 
Section&nbsp;4(e), if the Executive engages in any of the following conduct 
(termination for
&#147;<U>Cause</U>&#148;): </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; 
text-indent:13%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(i) the breaching 
of any material provision of this Agreement after the Company has given the 
Executive not
less than 30 days written notice of such breach and a period of not less than 30
days to correct, or cause to be corrected, such breach; </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:13%; font-size:10pt; 
font-family:Times New Roman">(ii) knowing and intentional misappropriation of 
funds or property of the Company or its affiliates; </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:13%; font-size:10pt;
font-family:Times New Roman">(iii) engaging in conduct, even if not in 
connection with the performance of the duties hereunder, which might be 
reasonably expected to
result in any effect materially adverse to the interests of the Company or any 
of its affiliates, such as fraud, dishonesty, conviction (or a judicial finding 
of evidence sufficient to convict) of any felony; </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P 
STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New 
Roman" ALIGN="right">Amended and Restated
Executive Employment Agreement </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt;

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:13%; font-size:10pt; 
font-family:Times New Roman">(iv) failing to fulfill and perform the duties 
assigned to the Executive in accordance with the
terms herein after the Company has given the Executive not less than 15 days 
written notice of such failure and a period of not less than 15 days to correct,
or cause to be corrected, such failure; and </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:13%; font-size:10pt; 
font-family:Times New Roman">(v) failing to comply with corporate policies of 
the Company or any of its affiliates that are promulgated from time to time by 
the Company,
<U>provided</U>, <U>however</U>, that the Company shall not be unreasonably 
arbitrary in its enforcement of corporate policies with respect to the 
Executive. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; 
font-family:Times New Roman">(b) <U>Termination by the Executive for Good 
Reason</U>. The Executive shall have good reason (&#147;<U>Good 
Reason</U>&#148;) as defined
below to resign his employment within sixty (60)&nbsp;days following notice and 
receive the same payments as provided under Section&nbsp;5(d) (and subject to 
the same release requirement), provided the Executive has first provided written
notice to
the Employer of conduct warranting termination of the Executive&#146;s 
employment for Good Reason and provided the Employer a period of not less than 
thirty (30)&nbsp;days to cure such conduct, without the written consent of the 
Executive: </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:13%; font-size:10pt; 
font-family:Times New Roman">(i) a material diminution in the nature and scope 
of the Executive&#146;s authorities or duties, including but not limited to a 
change in the
Executive&#146;s reporting relationship, a required move of more than a 50-mile 
radius of the Executive&#146;s employment prior to any such relocation, except 
for reasonably required travel on the Company&#146;s business or a reduction in 
pay (which
shall not be triggered by the Company&#146;s setting of the Executive Goals, 
beginning with the Company&#146;s 2017 fiscal year, pursuant Section&nbsp;4(c) 
above, even if the Executive&#146;s Annual Cash Award payout decreases as a 
result); or </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:13%; font-size:10pt; 
font-family:Times New Roman">(ii) a material breach of this Agreement by the 
Employer. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; 
font-family:Times New Roman">(c) <U>Termination by the Executive Without Good 
Reason</U>. The Executive may terminate his employment with the Company at any 
time, for any
reason, by providing 60 days&#146; advance written notice to the Company, which 
may be waived in whole or in part by the Company. If the Company waives the 
notice period in whole or in part, the Company shall pay the Base Salary for the
portion of
the notice period that has been waived. The Executive shall only be entitled to
payment of any accrued but unpaid Base Salary, accrued but unpaid out of pocket 
expenses in accordance with Section&nbsp;4(e) hereof and vacation pay accrued 
but unpaid
up to the Termination Date. The Executive shall not be entitled to any accrued 
annual bonus or other benefits. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-
bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(d) 
<U>Termination by the
Company Without Cause</U>. The Company may terminate the Executive&#146;s 
employment, without Cause as defined in Sections 5(a), in which case the Company
shall pay the Executive the following, less withholdings required by law: </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:13%; font-size:10pt; 
font-family:Times New Roman">(i) all accrued but unpaid Base Salary to the 
Termination Date; </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:13%; font-size:10pt; 
font-family:Times New Roman">(ii) all accrued but unpaid vacation pay to the 
Termination Date; </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:13%; font-size:10pt; 
font-family:Times New Roman">(iii) payment equal to the previous two 
(2)&nbsp;years&#146; bonuses paid to the Executive, plus a prorated portion of 
any bonus for the year
of the Executive&#146;s termination in an </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P

amount as provided under the applicable bonus plan of the Company, assuming a

<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:13%; font-size:10pt;

<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt;

in Section&nbsp;5(d) are inclusive of any termination and/or severance payments

<U>Change of Control</U>. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P 
STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New

Executive Employment Agreement </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt;

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:13%; font-size:10pt; 
font-family:Times New Roman">(i) Subject to Section&nbsp;5(e)(ii) below, within 
six (6)&nbsp;months following a Change of
Control of the Company, should the Company not renew or replace this Agreement 
with an Agreement containing substantially the same or better terms, the 
Executive shall be entitled to receive termination payments as set out in 
Section&nbsp;5(d) (but
subject to the requirement of a full and final release in favor of the Company 
in a form satisfactory to the Company), except that the 52-day period payment 
shall not apply, but instead the payment shall be made as a single lump 
immediately
following the expiration of a six (6)&nbsp;month period from the date the 
Executive elected to terminate his employment with the Company. For the purposes
of this Section&nbsp;5(e), &#147;Change of Control&#148; shall be defined as: 
(A)&nbsp;a
tender offer or exchange offer is made and consummated for the ownership of at 
least fifty percent (50%)&nbsp;of the outstanding voting securities of the 
Company; (B)&nbsp;the Company is merged or consolidated with another entity and 
as a result of
such merger or consolidation, at least fifty percent (50%)&nbsp;of the 
outstanding voting securities of the surviving or resulting entity is owned 
directly or indirectly in the aggregate by a person or persons other than a 
person or persons who
owned at least fifty percent (50%)&nbsp;of the outstanding voting securities of 
the Company immediately prior to such merger or consolidation; (C)&nbsp;the 
Company is liquidated or otherwise sells or transfers all or substantially all 
of its assets
to another entity which is not wholly owned, directly or indirectly, by a person
or persons who own at least fifty percent (50%)&nbsp;or more of the outstanding 
voting securities of the Company; or (D)&nbsp;a person, within the meaning of
Section&nbsp;3(a)(9) or Section&nbsp;13(d)(3) of the Securities Exchange Act of 
1934, as amended and in effect from time to time, acquires over fifty percent 
(50%)&nbsp;or more of the outstanding voting securities of the Company (whether 
directly,
indirectly, beneficially or of record). </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-
bottom:0pt; text-indent:13%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(ii) 
Notwithstanding Section&nbsp;5(e)(i) hereof to the contrary, the Executive 
acknowledges and
agrees that the Executive has waived such provision and the corresponding 
provision under Section&nbsp;5(e) of the Original Employment Agreement and any 
right to claim any such compensation and benefits provided under this Agreement 
in connection
therewith with respect to the transactions specified in the RSA (the 
&#147;<U>Restructuring Transactions</U>&#148;), and further acknowledges and 
agrees that the Restructuring Transactions shall not be considered a Change of 
Control under this
Section&nbsp;5(e) or under Section&nbsp;5(e) of the Original Employment 
Agreement. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; 
font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(f) <U>Death</U>. The 
Executive&#146;s employment with
the Company under this Agreement shall automatically terminate upon the death of
the Executive. Upon termination for death, the Executive or the Executive&#146;s
estate shall only be entitled to (i)&nbsp;payment of any portion of the Base 
Salary due
and owing up to such date; (ii)&nbsp;payment of any accrued but unused vacation 
pay; (iii)&nbsp;reimbursement of all out of pocket expenses in accordance with 
Section&nbsp;4(e); and (iv)&nbsp;notwithstanding any provision of any 
outstanding equity
award agreements that might otherwise be to the contrary, immediate acceleration
of all unvested outstanding equity awards under the Equity Incentive Plan or any
equity incentive plan or long term incentive plan of the Company, such that all
outstanding equity awards which have not already vested, shall immediately vest 
as of the Termination Date. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; 
text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(g) <U>Permanent
Disability</U>. In the event that the Executive suffers a Permanent Disability 
(as defined below), the employment of the Executive may be terminated by the 
Company upon 90 days&#146; notice to the Executive; except that if the 
termination of the
Executive&#146;s employment would impair his ability to receive long term 
disability benefits in whole or in part, </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P 
STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New 
Roman" ALIGN="right">Amended and Restated
Executive Employment Agreement </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt;
font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="right">Page 8 </P>

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times 
New Roman">
the Executive shall, in lieu of termination, be placed on an unpaid leave of 
absence, it being understood, however, that the Executive shall not be entitled
to re-employment by the Company after
such leave of absence or when he ceases to be in receipt of such benefits. Upon 
termination of employment for Permanent Disability, the Executive or the 
Executive&#146;s estate shall only be entitled to (i)&nbsp;payment of any 
portion of the Base
Salary due and owing up to such date; (ii)&nbsp;reimbursement of all expenses in
accordance with Section&nbsp;4(e); (iii)&nbsp;payment for any accrued but unused
vacation pay; and (iv)&nbsp;notwithstanding any provision of any outstanding 
equity
award agreements that might otherwise be to the contrary, immediate acceleration
of all unvested outstanding equity awards under the Equity Incentive Plan or any
equity incentive plan or long term incentive plan of the Company, such that all
outstanding equity awards which have not already vested, shall immediately vest 
as of the Termination Date. For the purposes of this Section&nbsp;5(g), 
&#147;Permanent Disability&#148; means a mental or physical disability whereby 
the Executive:
</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:13%; font-
size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(i) is unable, due to illness, disease, 
mental or physical disability or similar cause, to fulfill his obligations as an
employee or
officer of the Company either for three consecutive months or for a cumulative 
period of 6 months out of 12 consecutive calendar months, or </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:13%; font-size:10pt; 
font-family:Times New Roman">(ii) is declared by a court of competent 
jurisdiction to be mentally incompetent or incapable of managing his affairs. 
</P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; 
font-family:Times New Roman">(h) <U>Resignation as Officer or Director Upon 
Termination</U>. Upon termination of his employment for any reason whatsoever, 
the Executive
shall thereupon be deemed to have immediately resigned any position the 
Executive may have as an officer or director of the Company together with any 
other office, position or directorship which the Executive may hold with any of 
its affiliates. In
such event, the Executive shall, at the request of the Company, forthwith 
execute any and all documents appropriate to evidence such resignations. The 
Executive shall not be entitled to any payments in respect of such resignations 
in addition to
those provided for herein. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; 
text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(i) 
<U>Survival</U>. Notwithstanding the termination of the Executive&#146;s 
employment, or the manner of
termination, the provisions of Sections 6 and 7 of this Agreement and the Non-
Disclosure Agreement shall survive such termination. </P> <P STYLE="margin-
top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times 
New Roman">6.
<U>Non-Disclosure/Confidentiality Obligations</U>. The parties contemplate the 
Executive providing executive services to the Company in connection with its 
core business of providing effective acquisition of seismic data (the
&#147;<U>Business</U>&#148;). To facilitate the Executive&#146;s ability to 
perform these services, the Company agrees to provide the Executive 
confidential, proprietary, trade secret information regarding the Company&#146;s
business strategies,
plans, techniques and processes, which are more fully set forth in the Non-
Disclosure Agreement (&#147;<U>Confidential Information</U>&#148;), which the 
Company uses to compete in the marketplace, and the Executive agrees not to use 
or disclose such
Confidential Information for any purpose other than to advance the 
Company&#146;s interests. Moreover, from time to time, subsidiary companies or 
affiliates of the Company may provide that entity&#146;s confidential, 
proprietary information which
the Company uses to compete in the marketplace, to the Executive to facilitate 
the Executive&#146;s ability to provide services to the subsidiary companies or 
affiliates, and the Executive agrees not to use or disclose such Confidential
Information
for any purpose other than to advance the subsidiary companies&#146; or 
affiliate&#146;s interests. </P>

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; 
font-family:Times New Roman">7. <U>Post-Employment Obligations</U>. During the 
Term of this Agreement and for twelve
(12)&nbsp;months following the Termination Date: </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt;
margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New 
Roman">(a) the Executive will not, as a competitor or on behalf of any 
competitor of the
Company, directly or indirectly solicit or accept Business from any Customer (as
defined in the Non-Disclosure Agreement): (i)&nbsp;with whom the Executive had 
contact as a result of his duties with the Company or its affiliates, and/or
(ii)&nbsp;about whom the Executive reviewed or obtained Confidential Information
(as defined in the Non-Disclosure Agreement) while performing services for the 
Company or its affiliates. The geographic limitation for this restriction is 
(1)&nbsp;any
Company or its affiliates&#146; territory in which the Executive had a customer 
or service assignment for the Company or its affiliates in the twelve 
(12)&nbsp;month period immediately preceding the Executive&#146;s Termination 
Date; and/or
(2)&nbsp;any territory in which the Company or its affiliates, have customers or
service assignments about which the Executive obtained Confidential Information 
during the term of this Agreement; and </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; 
font-family:Times New Roman">(b) the Executive will not solicit, induce or 
attempt to induce any other employee, agent or contractor of the Company or its 
affiliates with
whom the Executive worked or about whom the Executive obtained Confidential 
Information in the twelve (12)&nbsp;month period immediately preceding the 
Executive&#146;s Termination Date, to leave the employ of the Company or its 
affiliates to work
for a competitor of the Company or its affiliates in the same or similar 
capacity as the other employee, agent or contractor of the Company or its 
affiliates worked for the Company or its affiliates. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; 
font-family:Times New Roman">(c) At the option of the Company, and in its sole 
discretion, the Company on the Termination Date may elect to extend the 
provisions of
Section&nbsp;7(a) and (b)&nbsp;for an additional twelve (12)&nbsp;months, in 
which case, the Company will pay to the Executive an amount equal to twelve 
(12)&nbsp;months of Base Salary as in effect at the Termination Date plus the 
Executive&#146;s
annual performance cash award under Section&nbsp;4(c) hereof at the 
Executive&#146;s Target Percentage of 75%, which shall be paid at the same time 
as the lump sum cash payment is made pursuant to Section&nbsp;5(b), 5(d) or 
5(e), as applicable, or,
in the absence of such a payment, within 52 days following the Termination Date,
in exchange for the Executive&#146;s continued compliance with the provisions of
Section&nbsp;7(a) and (b)&nbsp;for such additional twelve-month period. </P>

Agreement in their entirety. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt;

OF ANY CLAIM OR
CAUSE OF ACTION BASED UPON OR ARISING OUT OR RELATED TO THIS AGREEMENT IN ANY 
ACTION, PROCEEDING OR OTHER LITIGATION OF ANY TYPE BROUGHT BY ANY OF THE PARTIES
AGAINST ANY OTHER PARTY OR ANY AFFILIATE OF ANY OTHER SUCH PARTY, WHETHER WITH 
RESPECT TO
CONTRACT CLAIMS, TORT CLAIMS OR OTHERWISE. THE EMPLOYER AND THE EXECUTIVE EACH 
AGREE THAT ANY SUCH CLAIM OR CAUSE OF ACTION SHALL BE TRIED BY A COURT TRIAL 
WITHOUT A JURY. WITHOUT LIMITING THE FOREGOING, THE PARTIES FURTHER AGREE THAT 
THEIR
RESPECTIVE RIGHT TO A TRIAL BY JURY IS WAIVED BY OPERATION OF THIS SECTION AS TO
ANY ACTION, COUNTERCLAIM OR OTHER PROCEEDING WHICH SEEKS, IN WHOLE OR IN PART, 
TO CHALLENGE THE VALIDITY OR ENFORCEABILITY OF THIS AGREEMENT OR ANY PROVISION 
HEREOF.
THIS WAIVER SHALL APPLY TO ANY SUBSEQUENT AMENDMENTS, RENEWALS, SUPPLEMENTS OR 
MODIFICATIONS TO THIS AGREEMENT. </P>

font-family:Times New Roman">25. <U>Section&nbsp;409A</U>. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; 
font-family:Times New Roman">(a) To the extent applicable, this Agreement shall 
be interpreted and administered in a manner so that any amount or benefit 
payable shall be
paid or provided in a manner that is either exempt from or compliant with the 
requirements of Section&nbsp;409A of the Internal Revenue Code of 1986, as 
amended, and applicable guidance and regulations issued thereunder
(&#147;<U>Section
409A</U>&#148;). The parties agree to work together in good faith in an effort 
to comply with Section&nbsp;409A and any provision that would cause this 
Agreement to fail to satisfy Section&nbsp;409A shall have no force and effect 
until amended to
comply therewith (which amendment may be retroactive to the extent permitted by 
Section&nbsp;409A). In addition, for purposes of this Agreement, each amount to 
be paid or benefit to be provided to the Executive pursuant to this Agreement 
shall be
construed as a separate identified payment for purposes of Section&nbsp;409A.

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; 
font-family:Times New Roman">(b) With respect to any amount of expenses eligible
for reimbursement under this Agreement, such
expenses shall be reimbursed by the Company within thirty (30)&nbsp;days 
following the date on which the Company receives the applicable documentation 
from the Executive in accordance with its expense reimbursement policies, but in
no event later
than the last day of the Executive&#146;s taxable year following the taxable 
year in which the Executive incurs the related expenses. In no event shall the 
reimbursements or in-kind benefits to be provided under this Agreement in one 
taxable year
affect the amount of reimbursements or in-kind benefits to be provided in any 
other taxable year, nor will the Executive&#146;s right to reimbursement or in-
kind benefits be subject to liquidation or exchange for another benefit. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; 
font-family:Times New Roman">(c) Notwithstanding any provision to the contrary 
in this Agreement, if the Executive is deemed as of the Executive&#146;s 
Termination Date to
be a &#147;Specified Employee&#148; within the meaning of that term under Code 
Section&nbsp;409A(a)(2)(B), then with regard to any payment or the provision of 
any benefit that is required to be delayed in compliance with Code
Section&nbsp;409A(a)(2)(B), such payment or benefit (the &#147;Delayed 
Payment&#148;) shall not be made or provided prior to the earlier of 
(i)&nbsp;the first business day of the seventh month measured from the date of 
the Executive&#146;s
separation from service (within the meaning of Section&nbsp;409A or 
(ii)&nbsp;the date of the Executive&#146;s death (the &#147;<U>Delay 
Period</U>&#148;). Upon the expiration of the Delay Period (the 
&#147;<U>Permissible Payment Date</U>&#148;),
all Delayed Payments (whether they would have otherwise been payable in a single
sum or in installments in the absence of such delay) shall be paid or reimbursed
to the Executive in a lump sum on the Permissible Payment Date, and any 
remaining
payments and benefits due under this Agreement shall be paid or provided in 
accordance with the normal payment dates specified for them herein. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; 
font-family:Times New Roman">26. <U>Counsel</U>. The Executive acknowledges that
he is executing a legal document that contains certain duties, obligations and
restrictions as specified herein. The Executive furthermore acknowledges that he
has been advised of his right to retain legal counsel, and that he has either 
been represented by legal counsel prior to his execution hereof or has knowingly
elected
not to be so represented. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; 
text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">By signing below,
the Executive acknowledges that he has received, read, and agrees to adhere to 
the terms and
conditions contained within this Agreement. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; 
margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" 
ALIGN="center">[Signatures on the following page] </P>

 <BODY BGCOLOR="WHITE">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times 
New Roman" ALIGN="right"><B>Exhibit 10.4 </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times 
New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B><U>AMENDED AND RESTATED EXECUTIVE EMPLOYMENT 
AGREEMENT </U></B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times 
New Roman">THIS AMENDED AND RESTATED EXECUTIVE EMPLOYMENT AGREEMENT (the 
&#147;<U>Agreement</U>&#148;), effective as of the Effective Date (as defined 
below), is entered
into by and between SAExploration Holdings, Inc., a Delaware corporation (the 
&#147;<U>Employer</U>&#148; or the &#147;<U>Company</U>&#148;), and <U>Mike 
Scott</U>, an individual residing in the Province of Alberta, Canada (the
&#147;<U>Executive</U>&#148;) and amends, restates and replaces in its entirety 
the Executive Employment Agreement dated as of October&nbsp;1st 2012, other than
the provisions of the Non-Disclosure Agreement (as such term is defined herein) 
(the
&#147;<U>Original Employment Agreement</U>&#148;). The Employer and the 
Executive may be referred to singularly as &#147;<U>Party</U>&#148; or 
collectively as &#147;<U>Parties</U>.&#148; Unless otherwise specified, 
capitalized terms have the
meanings set forth herein. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:24pt; margin-bottom:0pt; 
font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><U>RECITALS </U></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; 
font-family:Times New Roman">WHEREAS, the Company and certain of its 
subsidiaries and such other parties identified therein entered into that certain
Restructuring Support
Agreement dated as of June&nbsp;13, 2016, whereby the parties thereto have 
agreed to enter into certain transactions that will have the effect of 
restructuring and recapitalizing the Company (the &#147;<U>RSA</U>&#148;) 
effective upon the Closing
Date (as such term is defined in the RSA); </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; 
margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New 
Roman">WHEREAS, prior to the Effective Date, the Employer has employed the 
Executive as Executive
Vice President&#151;Operations of the Company; </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; 
margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New 
Roman">WHEREAS, in connection with and pursuant to the provisions of the RSA, 
the Parties have
agreed to amend the Original Employment Agreement on the terms and conditions 
contained herein effective immediately upon the date of approval (the
&#147;<U>Effective Date</U>&#148;) by the Board of Directors of the Company (the
&#147;<U>Board</U>&#148;); </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; 
text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">WHEREAS, effective 
immediately upon the Effective Date, the Company will employ the Executive as 
the Senior
Vice President of the Company, and the Executive desires to be employed by the 
Employer on the terms and conditions contained herein; </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; 
font-family:Times New Roman">WHEREAS, the Employer acknowledges and rewards the 
value and loyalty of the Executive and seeks to build and protect the 
Company&#146;s
stability, growth, customer base, technology and other competitive advantages; 
and </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-
size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">WHEREAS, the Executive wishes to 
evidence his
commitment to the Company and its objectives. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; 
margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New 
Roman">NOW, THEREFORE, in consideration of the foregoing premises and the 
respective agreements
hereinafter set forth and the mutual benefits to be derived hereinafter, the 
Employer and the Executive hereby agree as follows: </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:24pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times 
New Roman" ALIGN="center"><U>AGREEMENTS </U></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; 
margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New 
Roman">1.
<U>Employment Term</U>. The Employer hereby agrees to continue to employ the 
Executive commencing on the Effective Date and ending on the third anniversary 
thereafter (the &#147;<U>Initial Term</U>&#148;); <U>provided</U>, 
<U>however</U>, that at
the end of the Initial Term, the Executive&#146;s </P>
<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times 
New Roman">
employment and this Agreement shall automatically renew or extend for 
consecutive terms of one (1)&nbsp;year on each succeeding anniversary of the 
Effective Date (each such renewal or extension a
&#147;<U>Renewal Term</U>&#148;), unless either Party gives prior written notice
to the other Party of its desire to terminate the Agreement at least 90 days 
prior to the expiration of the Initial Term or any Renewal Term, as applicable 
(the Initial
Term and each Renewal Term, collectively, the &#147;<U>Term</U>&#148;). 
Notwithstanding the foregoing, the Parties shall have the termination rights as 
set forth in Section&nbsp;5 of this Agreement. Termination of this Agreement for
any reason
whatsoever by any Party shall have no effect on the continued enforceability of 
any ancillary agreement, specifically including the Non-Disclosure Agreement 
executed by the Executive in favor of the Employer concurrently with the 
Original Employment
Agreement, (the &#147;<U>Non-Disclosure Agreement</U>&#148;). The obligations of
the Parties under Sections 5 through 27 shall survive according to the terms of 
each provision. The Executive accepts such continued employment and agrees to 
continue
to perform the services specified herein, all upon the terms and conditions 
hereinafter stated. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-
indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">2. <U>Duties</U>. During
the Term, the
Executive shall serve in the position of Senior Vice President of the Company 
and shall report to and be subject to the general direction and control of the 
Chief Executive Officer of the Company (the &#147;<U>CEO</U>&#148;) or the 
CEO&#146;s
designee. In such capacity he shall be responsible for the supervision of the 
day to day operations of the Company and the implementation of its business
plans and strategies, in each case, subject to the CEO and in accordance with 
and subject to
budgets approved from time to time by such CEO. The Executive shall perform such
duties consistent with the Executive&#146;s position, as well as other duties 
from time to time assigned to the Executive by the CEO. The Executive further 
agrees to
perform, without additional compensation, such other services for the Employer 
and for any of its affiliates as the Board shall from time to time specify, if 
such services are of the nature commonly associated with or similar to that of 
the
Executive&#146;s position with a company engaged in activities similar to the 
activities engaged in by the Employer at the time of execution of this 
Agreement. For purposes of the Non-Disclosure Agreement and Sections 5 through 
27, the term
&#147;Employer&#148; shall be deemed to include and refer to any and all 
affiliates of the Employer. The Executive acknowledges and agrees that the Non-
Disclosure Agreement executed simultaneously with the Original Employment 
Agreement is hereby
incorporated by reference herein and made a part hereof and that the Non-
Disclosure Agreement constitutes a material part of this Agreement. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; 
font-family:Times New Roman">3. <U>Extent of Service</U>. The Executive shall 
devote his full business time, attention, and energy to the business of the 
Employer, and
shall not be engaged in any other business activity that competes with or 
detracts from the business of the Employer during the Term of this Agreement. 
The foregoing shall not be construed as preventing the Executive from making 
passive investments
in other businesses or enterprises, if (i)&nbsp;such investments will not 
require services on the part of the Executive which would in any material way 
impair the performance of his duties under this Agreement, or (ii)&nbsp;such 
other businesses or
enterprises are not engaged in any business competitive with the business of the
Employer or any of its affiliates. The Executive shall be based in the vicinity 
of the Calgary metropolitan area (or such other area as may be agreed upon by 
the
Parties) and, subject to travel requirements as reasonably necessary to support 
successful business development efforts and management of the business, shall 
perform his services from a mutually agreed location in that area. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P 
STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New 
Roman" ALIGN="right">Amended and Restated
Executive Employment Agreement </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt;
font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="right">Page 2 </P>
<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; 
font-family:Times New Roman">4. <U>Compensation and Benefits</U>. As payment for
the services to be rendered by the Executive
hereunder during the Term of this Agreement, the Executive shall be entitled to 
the following: </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-
indent:8%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(a) receive payment of 
the
Executive&#146;s annual base salary at the rate of not less than US$333,716.00 a
year (the &#147;<U>Base Salary</U>&#148;), less deductions required by law, 
payable in accordance with the Employer&#146;s standard payroll schedule, but 
not less
frequently than monthly; <U>provided</U>, that commencing with the 
Company&#146;s 2017 fiscal year, the Executive&#146;s Base Salary may be 
increased annually (but not decreased without the written consent of the 
Executive) in the discretion of the
Board; </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-
size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(b) a monthly automobile allowance of 
US$1,750 per month payable in accordance with the Employer&#146;s standard 
payroll schedule,
and which shall be subject to customary deductions and withholding; </P> <P 
STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; font-
family:Times New Roman">(c) continue to be eligible to participate in any short-
term and
long-term incentive compensation plans, annual bonus plans and such other 
management incentive programs or arrangements of the Company approved by the 
Board that are generally available to the Company&#146;s senior executives and 
continue to be
eligible to receive annual performance cash awards (&#147;<U>Annual Cash 
Awards</U>&#148;) at the rate of 25% to 75% of Base Salary (the &#147;<U>Target 
Percentage</U>&#148;), and the Executive will be entitled to a guaranteed 25% 
annual performance
cash award and as much as 75% if certain executive goals (the &#147;<U>Executive
Goals</U>&#148;) are reached as identified and approved by the Compensation 
Committee of the Board (the &#147;<U>Compensation Committee</U>&#148;), but not 
to exceed
the maximum award permissible under the applicable long-term incentive plan for 
such annual award; <U>provided</U>, that, at the option of the Compensation 
Committee, up to 50% of any Annual Cash Award payable to the Executive may be 
paid in shares
of the Company&#146;s common stock (which is in addition to any shares of the 
Company&#146;s common stock reserved for issuance under the SAExploration 
Holdings, Inc. 2016 Long-Term Incentive Plan, as may be amended, restated and 
supplemented from
time to time (the &#147;<U>Equity Incentive Plan</U>&#148;)); <U>provided</U>, 
<U>further</U>, that such Target Percentage will be applied to twelve 
(12)&nbsp;times the highest paid monthly base salary within the applicable 
calendar year. Commencing
with the Company&#146;s 2017 fiscal year, the Executive Goals will be set by the
Compensation Committee under the applicable long-term incentive plan for such 
annual award but in any event shall not exceed the maximum award permissible 
under such
applicable plan; </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-
indent:8%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(d) the Executive will 
be entitled to participate, on the same basis generally as other similarly 
situated employees of
the Company, in all benefits as may be offered by the Company from time to time;
</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-
size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(e) reimbursement of reasonable expenses
incurred by the
Executive in accordance with such expense reimbursement policies of the Company;
and </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-
size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(f) paid vacation of six (6)&nbsp;weeks 
per year.
</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-
size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(g) <U>Equity Compensation</U>. The 
Executive shall be eligible to participate in the Equity Incentive Plan and such
other equity
incentive programs or arrangements of the Company approved by the Board that are
generally available to the Company&#146;s senior executives. The </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P 
STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New 
Roman" ALIGN="right">Amended and Restated
Executive Employment Agreement </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt;
font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="right">Page 3 </P>
<p Style='page-break-before:always'>

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times 
New Roman">
Board or the Compensation Committee, as applicable, pursuant to written 
corporate action taken or at a meeting held, in either case, shall, effective on
September&nbsp;26, 2016 (the
&#147;<U>Grant Date</U>&#148;), subject to the Executive&#146;s employment on 
such Grant Date, award to the Executive the following: </P> <P STYLE="margin-
top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:13%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times 
New Roman">(i)
<U>Stock Units</U>. 33,743 Stock Units (as such term is defined in the Equity 
Incentive Plan) under the Equity Incentive Plan (the &#147;<U>MIP RSU 
Grant</U>&#148;) pursuant to a Stock Units Agreement (as such term is defined in
the Equity Incentive
Plan) that will provide for vesting of the MIP RSU Grant in equal installments, 
subject to the Executive&#146;s continued employment, except as otherwise 
specified, as follows: </P>
