for the 30-day period that ends on the Grant Date, and will provide for vesting

 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">the remaining one-third (1/3)&nbsp;of the MIP

<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; 
font-family:Times New Roman"><U>provided</U>, <U>however</U>, that if the 
Executive&#146;s employment is terminated by reason of the Executive&#146;s: 
(i)&nbsp;death;
(ii)&nbsp;Permanent Disability; (iii)&nbsp;termination by the Company other than
for Cause; or (iv)&nbsp;termination for Good Reason, all unvested portions of 
the Executive&#146;s MIP RSU Grant and the MIP Option Grant shall become fully 
vested upon
such termination. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-
indent:13%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(iii) For the avoidance
of doubt, the vesting of any awards granted to the Executive under the Equity 
Incentive Plan
shall not be conditioned on any financial, operating or other performance 
metrics. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; 
font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(h) Notwithstanding any other 
provisions in this
Agreement to the contrary, any incentive-based compensation, or any other 
compensation, paid to the Executive pursuant to this Agreement or any other 
agreement or arrangement with the Company which is subject to recovery under any
law, governmental
regulation or stock exchange listing requirement or policy of the Company 
adopted to comply with any such law, regulation, or listing requirement, will be
subject to such deductions and requirements for repayment 
(&#147;<U>Clawback</U>&#148;) as may
be required to be made pursuant to such law, governmental regulation, stock 
exchange listing requirement, or policy. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-
bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(i) 
Notwithstanding
any provisions in this Agreement, the Equity Incentive Plan or any award 
agreement evidencing the grants set forth in Section&nbsp;4(g) above to the 
contrary, if the Executive terminates his employment for any reason other than 
Good Reason prior to
the first anniversary of the Closing Date, any awards granted pursuant to 
Section&nbsp;4(g) (whether vested or unvested) will be automatically forfeited, 
and the Executive will be required to return and/or repay any shares or cash 
proceeds received
in respect of such awards. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; 
text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">5. 
<U>Termination</U>. This Agreement and the Executive&#146;s employment with the 
Company may be terminated
in accordance with this Section&nbsp;5. The date upon which any such termination
becomes effective shall be deemed the &#147;Termination Date.&#148; </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; 
font-family:Times New Roman">(a) <U>Termination by the Company for Cause</U>. 
The Company may terminate this Agreement and Executive&#146;s employment with 
the Company at
any time without notice and without any payment to the Executive whatsoever, 
save and except for the payment of any Base Salary, vacation accrued but unpaid 
up to the Termination Date and out of pocket expenses in accordance with 
Section&nbsp;4(e),
if the Executive engages in any of the following conduct (termination for 
&#147;Cause&#148;): </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-
indent:13%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(i) the breaching of 
any material
provision of this Agreement after Company has given the Executive reasonable 
notice of such breach and a reasonable opportunity to correct, or cause to be 
corrected, such breach; </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:13%; font-size:10pt; 
font-family:Times New Roman">(ii) knowing and intentional misappropriation of 
funds or property of the Company or its affiliates; </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P 
STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New 
Roman" ALIGN="right">Amended and Restated
Executive Employment Agreement </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt;
font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="right">Page 5 </P>
<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:13%; font-size:10pt; 
font-family:Times New Roman">(iii) engaging in conduct, even if not in 
connection with the performance of the duties
hereunder, which might be reasonably expected to result in any effect materially
adverse to the interests of the Company or any of its affiliates, such as fraud,
dishonesty, conviction (or a judicial finding of evidence sufficient to convict)
of any
felony; </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:13%; 
font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(iv) failing to fulfill and perform
the duties assigned to the Executive in accordance with the terms hereto after 
the Company
has given the Executive reasonable notice of such failure and a reasonable 
opportunity to correct, or cause to be corrected, such failure; </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:13%; font-size:10pt; 
font-family:Times New Roman">(v) failing to comply with corporate policies of 
the Company or any of its affiliates that are promulgated from time to time by 
the Company,
<U>provided</U>, <U>however</U>, that the Company shall not be unreasonably 
arbitrary in its enforcement of corporate policies with respect to the 
Executive; </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:13%; font-size:10pt; 
font-family:Times New Roman">(vi) death of the Executive; and </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:13%; font-size:10pt; 
font-family:Times New Roman">(vii) disability of the Executive which prevents 
the Executive from performing the essential functions of the position assigned 
under this
Agreement, with or without reasonable accommodation. Disability status under
this Agreement will be consistent with the disability and leave procedures 
promulgated from time to time by the Company. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; 
font-family:Times New Roman">(b) <U>Termination by the Executive for Good 
Reason</U>. The Executive shall have good reason (&#147;<U>Good 
Reason</U>&#148;) as defined
below to resign his employment within sixty (60)&nbsp;days following notice and 
receive the payments as provided under Section&nbsp;6 (and subject to the same 
release requirement), provided the Executive has first provided written notice 
to the
Employer of conduct warranting termination of the Executive&#146;s employment 
for Good Reason and provided the Employer a period of not less than thirty 
(30)&nbsp;days to cure such conduct, without the written consent of the 
Executive: </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:13%; font-size:10pt; 
font-family:Times New Roman">(i) a material diminution in the nature and scope 
of the Executive&#146;s authorities or duties, including but not limited to a 
change in the
Executive&#146;s reporting relationship, a required move of more than a 50-mile 
radius of the Executive&#146;s employment prior to any such relocation, except 
for reasonably required travel on the Company&#146;s business or a reduction in 
pay (which
shall not be triggered by the Company&#146;s setting of the Executive Goals, 
beginning with the Company&#146;s 2017 fiscal year, pursuant Section&nbsp;4(c) 
above, even if the Executive&#146;s Annual Cash Award payout decreases as a 
result); or </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:13%; font-size:10pt; 
font-family:Times New Roman">(ii) a material breach of this Agreement by the 
Employer. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; 
font-family:Times New Roman">(c) <U>Termination by the Executive Without Good 
Reason</U>. The Executive may terminate his employment with the Company at any 
time, for any
reason, by providing 60 days&#146; advance written notice to the Company, which 
may be waived in whole or in part by the Company. If the Company waives the 
notice period in whole or in part, the Company shall pay the Base Salary for the
portion of
the notice period that has been waived. The Executive shall only be entitled to 
payment of any accrued but unpaid Base Salary, accrued but unpaid out of pocket 
expenses in accordance with Section&nbsp;4(e) hereof and vacation pay accrued 
but unpaid
up to the Termination Date. The Executive shall not be entitled to any accrued 
annual bonus or other benefits. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P 
STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New 
Roman" ALIGN="right">Amended and Restated
Executive Employment Agreement </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt;
font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="right">Page 6 </P>
<p Style='page-break-before:always'>

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; 
font-family:Times New Roman">(d) <U>Termination by the Company Without 
Cause</U>. The Company may terminate the
Executive&#146;s employment without Cause. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; 
margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New 
Roman">(e) <U>Termination by Change of Control</U>. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:13%; font-size:10pt; 
font-family:Times New Roman">(i) Subject to Section&nbsp;5(e)(ii) below, within 
six (6)&nbsp;months following a Change of Control of the Company, should the 
Company not
renew or replace this Agreement with an Agreement containing substantially the 
same or better terms, the Executive shall be entitled to receive termination
payments as set out in Section&nbsp;6 (but subject to the requirement of a full 
and final
release in favor of the Company in a form satisfactory to the Company), except 
that the 15-day period payment shall not apply, but instead the payment shall be
made as a single lump immediately following the expiration of a six 
(6)&nbsp;month period
from the date the Executive elected to terminate his employment with the 
Company. &#147;Change of Control&#148; shall mean such time as any of the 
following occur after the date of this Agreement: (i)&nbsp;a tender offer or 
exchange offer is made
and consummated for the ownership of fifty-one percent (51%)&nbsp;of the 
outstanding voting securities of the Company, (ii)&nbsp;the Company is merged or
consolidated with another entity and as a result of such merger or consolidation
fifty-one
percent (51%)&nbsp;of the outstanding voting securities of the surviving or 
resulting entity is owned directly or indirectly in the aggregate by a person or
persons other than a person or persons who owned fifty one percent (51%)&nbsp;of
the
outstanding voting securities of the Company immediately prior to such merger or
consolidation, (iii)&nbsp;the Company is liquidated or otherwise sells or 
transfers all or substantially all of its assets to another entity which is not 
wholly owned,
directly or indirectly, by a person or persons who own fifty percent 
(50%)&nbsp;or more of the outstanding voting securities of the Company, or 
(iv)&nbsp;a person, within the meaning of Section&nbsp;3(a)(9) or 
Section&nbsp;13(d)(3) of the Securities
Exchange Act of 1934, as amended and in effect from time to time, acquires over 
fifty one percent (51%)&nbsp;or more of the outstanding voting securities of the
Company (whether directly, indirectly, beneficially or of record). </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:13%; font-size:10pt; 
font-family:Times New Roman">(ii) Notwithstanding Section&nbsp;5(e)(i) hereof to
the contrary, the Executive acknowledges and agrees that the Executive has 
waived such
provision and the corresponding provision under Section&nbsp;5(d) of the 
Original Employment Agreement and any right to claim any such compensation and 
benefits provided under this Agreement in connection therewith with respect to 
the transactions
specified in the RSA (the &#147;<U>Restructuring Transactions</U>&#148;), and 
further acknowledges and agrees that the Restructuring Transactions shall not be
considered a Change of Control under this Section&nbsp;5(e) or under 
Section&nbsp;5(d) of
the Original Employment Agreement. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-
bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">6. 
<U>Payments Upon Termination</U>. In the event this Agreement and the 
Executive&#146;s employment
with the Company is terminated by the Executive with Good Reason under 
Section&nbsp;5(b), by the Company without Cause under Section&nbsp;5(d) or by 
the Executive under the circumstances described under Section&nbsp;5(e), the 
Executive shall be
entitled to: </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; 
font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(a) all accrued but unpaid Base 
Salary to the Termination Date; </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P 
STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New 
Roman" ALIGN="right">Amended and Restated
Executive Employment Agreement </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt;
font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="right">Page 7 </P>
<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; 
font-family:Times New Roman">(b) all accrued but unpaid vacation pay to the 
Termination Date; </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; 
font-family:Times New Roman">(c) payment equal to twenty-four 
(24)&nbsp;months&#146; Base Salary; </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; 
font-family:Times New Roman">(d) payment equal to the previous two 
(2)&nbsp;years&#146; bonuses paid to the Executive, plus a prorated portion of 
any bonus for the year of
the Executive&#146;s termination in an amount as provided under the applicable 
bonus plan of the Company, assuming a payment at the Target Percentage of 100%. 
If a bonus payment was not paid to the Executive in any of those previous two
(2)&nbsp;years, the amount for this section will be calculated on the assumption
that the bonus paid for any unpaid year was paid at the Target Percentage of 
100%; and </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; 
font-family:Times New Roman">(e) five percent (5%)&nbsp;of the amount paid 
pursuant to Section&nbsp;6(a) as compensation for the loss of employment 
benefits. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times 
New Roman">Prior to, and as a condition to, receiving the payments in 
Section&nbsp;6 (other than payments pursuant to Sections 6(a) and (b)), the 
Executive agrees to
execute a full and final release in favor of the Company, in a form satisfactory
to the Company, not later than fifteen (15)&nbsp;days following the Termination 
Date. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times 
New Roman">The above amounts will be paid in a single lump sum not later than 
fifteen (15)&nbsp;days of the Termination Date subject to the fulfillment of the
provision
of a full and final release,<U> provided</U>, <U>however</U>, if such 15-day 
period begins in one taxable year and ends in a second taxable year, the payment
date shall be deemed to be the later of (i)&nbsp;the first business day in the 
year
following the year in which the Executive&#146;s &#147;separation from 
service&#148; occurs or (ii)&nbsp;the last day of such 15-day period. The 
payments referred to in this Section&nbsp;6 shall not be subject to the 
requirement of mitigation, nor
reduced by any actual mitigation by the Executive and are inclusive of any 
termination and/or severance payments that may be required under employment 
standards legislation. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; 
font-family:Times New Roman">7. <U>Non-Disclosure/Confidentiality 
Obligations</U>. The parties contemplate the Executive providing executive 
services to the Company in
connection with its core business of providing effective acquisition of seismic 
data (the &#147;<U>Business</U>&#148;). To facilitate the Executive&#146;s 
ability to perform these services, the Company agrees to provide the Executive 
confidential,
proprietary, trade secret information regarding the Company&#146;s business 
strategies, plans, techniques and processes, which are more fully set forth in 
the Non-Disclosure Agreement (&#147;<U>Confidential Information</U>&#148;), 
which the Company
uses to compete in the marketplace, and the Executive agrees not to use or 
disclose such Confidential Information for any purpose other than to advance the
Company&#146;s interests. Moreover, from time to time, subsidiary companies or 
affiliates of
the Company may provide that entity&#146;s confidential, proprietary information
which the Company uses to compete in the marketplace, to the Executive to 
facilitate the Executive&#146;s ability to provide services to the subsidiary 
companies or
affiliates, and the Executive agrees not to use or disclose such Confidential 
Information for any purpose other than to advance the subsidiary companies&#146;
or affiliate&#146;s interests. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; 
font-family:Times New Roman">8. <U>Post-Employment Obligations</U>. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; 
font-family:Times New Roman">During the Term of this Agreement and for 12 months
following the Termination Date: </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P 
STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New 
Roman" ALIGN="right">Amended and Restated
Executive Employment Agreement </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt;
font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="right">Page 8 </P>
<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; 
font-family:Times New Roman">(a) the Executive will not, as a competitor or on 
behalf of any competitor of the Company,
directly or indirectly solicit or accept Business from any Customer (as defined 
in the Non-Disclosure Agreement): (i)&nbsp;with whom the Executive had contact 
as a result of his duties with the Company or its affiliates, and/or 
(ii)&nbsp;about whom
the Executive reviewed or obtained Confidential Information (as defined in the 
Non-Disclosure Agreement) while performing services for the Company or its 
affiliates. The geographic limitation for this restriction is (1)&nbsp;any 
Company or its
affiliates&#146; territory in which the Executive had a customer or service 
assignment for the Company or its affiliates in the twelve (12)&nbsp;month 
period immediately preceding the Executive&#146;s Termination Date; and/or 
(2)&nbsp;any territory
in which the Company or its affiliates, have customers or service assignments 
about which the Executive obtained Confidential Information during the term of 
this Agreement; and </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; 
font-family:Times New Roman">(b) the Executive will not solicit, induce or 
attempt to induce any other employee, agent or contractor of the Company or its 
affiliates with
whom the Executive worked or about whom the Executive obtained Confidential 
Information in the twelve (12)&nbsp;month period immediately preceding the 
Executive&#146;s Termination Date, to leave the employ of the Company or its 
affiliates to work
for a competitor of the Company or its affiliates in the same or similar 
capacity as the other employee, agent or contractor of the Company or its 
affiliates worked for the Company or its affiliates. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; 
font-family:Times New Roman">(c) At the option of the Company, and in its sole 
discretion, the Company on the Termination Date may elect to extend the 
provisions of
Section&nbsp;8(a) and (b)&nbsp;for an additional twelve (12)&nbsp;months, in 
which case, the Company will pay to the Executive an amount equal to twelve 
(12)&nbsp;months of Base Salary as in effect at the Termination Date plus the 
Executive&#146;s
annual performance cash award under Section&nbsp;4(c) hereof at the 
Executive&#146;s Target Percentage of 50%, which shall be paid at the same time 
as the lump sum cash payment is made pursuant to Section&nbsp;6, as applicable, 
or, in the absence of
such a payment, within 15 days following the Termination Date, in exchange for 
the Executive&#146;s continued compliance with the provisions of 
Section&nbsp;8(a) and (b)&nbsp;for such additional twelve-month period. </P>

font-family:Times New Roman">9. <U>Insurance</U>. </P> <P STYLE="margin-

<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt;

any of the under this Agreement in connection therewith with respect to the

available to it for such breach or threatened breach. If a bond is required to 
be posted in order for either Party to secure an injunction, then the Parties 
stipulate that a bond in the amount of One Thousand and No/100 Dollars 
(US$1,000) will be
sufficient and reasonable in all circumstances to protect the rights of the 
Parties. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; 
font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">12. <U>Severability</U>. Whenever 
possible, each
provision of this Agreement shall be interpreted in such manner as to be 
effective and valid under applicable law, but if any provision of this Agreement
shall be prohibited by or invalid under applicable law, such provisions shall be
ineffective to
the extent of such provision or invalidity only, without invalidating the 
remainder of such provision or any remaining provisions of this Agreement. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; 
font-family:Times New Roman">13. <U>Assignment</U>. This Agreement may not be 
assigned by the Executive. Neither the Executive, his spouse, nor their estates 
shall have
any right to encumber or dispose of any right to receive payments under this 
Agreement, it being understood that such payments and the right thereto are 
nonassignable and nontransferable. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; 
font-family:Times New Roman">14. <U>Binding Effect</U>. Subject to the 
provisions of Section&nbsp;13 above, this Agreement shall be binding upon and 
inure to the benefit
of the Parties hereto, the Executive&#146;s heirs and personal representatives, 
and the successors and assignees of the Employer. </P> <P STYLE="margin-
top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times 
New Roman">15.
<U>Prior Employment Agreements and Obligations</U>. The Executive represents and
warrants to the Employer that he has fulfilled all of the terms and conditions 
of all prior employment agreements and employer policies to which he may be a 
party or
have been a party, and that at the time of execution of this Agreement, the 
Executive is not a party to or otherwise restricted by any other employment 
agreement, non-solicitation agreement, non-competition covenant, confidentiality
or nondisclosure
agreement (other than the Non-Disclosure Agreement) in any manner which would 
prevent the Executive from performing the services contemplated by this 
Agreement. The Executive represents and warrants that nothing contained in any 
agreement that he
has with any parties shall preclude the Executive from performing all of his 
duties, </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P 
STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New 
Roman" ALIGN="right">Amended and Restated
Executive Employment Agreement </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt;
font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="right">Page 10 </P>
<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times 
New Roman">
obligations and covenants as contained in this Agreement. The Employer is 
entering into this Agreement solely for the expertise and experience of the 
Executive, and the Employer expressly forbids
the Executive from using or disclosing any confidential information or trade 
secrets of any prior employer or other third party in connection with the 
Executive&#146;s performance under this Agreement. The Executive represents and 
warrants to the
Employer that he has not and will not in the future, take, use or disclose the 
confidential information or trade secrets of a third-party for the benefit of 
the Employer. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; 
font-family:Times New Roman">16. <U>Parol Evidence</U>. This Agreement and the 
Non-Disclosure Agreement (and any other agreements incorporated by reference 
herein)
constitutes the sole and complete agreement between the Parties hereto as to the
matters contained herein, and no verbal or other statements, inducements or 
representations have been made to or relied upon by either Party, and no 
modification hereof
shall be effective unless in writing, signed, and executed in the same manner as
this Agreement; <U>provided</U>, <U>however</U>, that the amount of compensation
to be paid to the Executive for services to be performed for the Employer may be
changed from time to time by the Parties hereto by written agreement without in 
any other way modifying, changing, or affecting this Agreement and the 
performance by the Executive of any of the duties of his employment with the 
Employer. The
provisions of this Agreement supersede the provisions of the Original Employment
Agreement in their entirety. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; 
text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">17. <U>Waiver</U>. 
Any
waiver to be enforceable must be in writing and executed by the Party against 
whom the waiver is sought to be enforced. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; 
margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New 
Roman">18. <U>Governing
Law</U>. All issues and questions concerning the construction, validity, 
enforcement and interpretation of this Agreement shall be governed by, and 
construed in accordance with, the Province of Alberta, Canada, without giving 
effect to any choice of
law or conflict of law rules or provisions (whether of the Province of Alberta, 
Canada or any other jurisdiction) that would cause the application of the laws 
of any jurisdiction other than the Province of Alberta, Canada. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; 
font-family:Times New Roman">19. <U>Mutual Waiver of Jury Trial</U>. THE 
EMPLOYER AND THE EXECUTIVE EACH WAIVE THEIR RESPECTIVE RIGHT TO A TRIAL BY JURY 
OF ANY CLAIM OR
CAUSE OF ACTION BASED UPON OR ARISING OUT OR RELATED TO THIS AGREEMENT IN ANY 
ACTION, PROCEEDING OR OTHER LITIGATION OF ANY TYPE BROUGHT BY ANY OF THE PARTIES
AGAINST ANY OTHER PARTY OR ANY AFFILIATE OF ANY OTHER SUCH PARTY, WHETHER WITH 
RESPECT TO
CONTRACT CLAIMS, TORT CLAIMS OR OTHERWISE. THE EMPLOYER AND THE EXECUTIVE EACH 
AGREE THAT ANY SUCH CLAIM OR CAUSE OF ACTION SHALL BE TRIED BY A COURT TRIAL 
WITHOUT A JURY. WITHOUT LIMITING THE FOREGOING, THE PARTIES FURTHER AGREE THAT 
THEIR
RESPECTIVE RIGHT TO A TRIAL BY JURY IS WAIVED BY OPERATION OF THIS SECTION AS TO
ANY ACTION, COUNTERCLAIM OR OTHER PROCEEDING WHICH SEEKS, IN WHOLE OR IN PART, 
TO CHALLENGE THE VALIDITY OR ENFORCEABILITY OF THIS AGREEMENT OR ANY PROVISION 
HEREOF.
THIS WAIVER SHALL APPLY TO ANY SUBSEQUENT AMENDMENTS, RENEWALS, SUPPLEMENTS OR 
MODIFICATIONS TO THIS AGREEMENT. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P 
STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New 
Roman" ALIGN="right">Amended and Restated
Executive Employment Agreement </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt;

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; 
font-family:Times New Roman">20. <U>Attorneys&#146; Fees</U>. If any litigation 
is instituted to enforce or interpret the
provisions of this Agreement or the transactions described herein, the 
prevailing Party in such action shall be entitled to recover its reasonable 
attorneys&#146; fees from the other Party or Parties hereto. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; 
font-family:Times New Roman">21. <U>Drafting</U>. Each of the Parties hereto 
acknowledges that each Party was actively involved in the negotiation and 
drafting of this
Agreement and that no law or rule of construction shall be raised or used in 
which the provisions of this Agreement shall be construed in favor or against 
any Party hereto because one is deemed to be the author thereof. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; 
font-family:Times New Roman">22. <U>Multiple Counterparts</U>. This Agreement 
may be executed in multiple counterparts, including by facsimile transmission 
and email in
portable document format, each of which shall have the force and effect of an 
original, and all of which shall constitute one and the same agreement. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; 
font-family:Times New Roman">23. <U>Acknowledgment of Enforceability</U>. The 
Executive acknowledges and agrees that this Agreement contains reasonable 
limitations as to
time, geographical area, and scope of activity to be restrained that do not 
impose a greater restraint than is necessary to protect the goodwill or other 
business interest of the Employer. Therefore, the Executive agrees that all 
restrictions are
fairly compensated for and that no unreasonable restrictions exist. </P> <P 
STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-
family:Times New Roman">24. <U>Reconstruction of Agreement</U>. Should a court 
of competent
jurisdiction or an arbitrator having jurisdiction declare any of the provisions 
of this Agreement unenforceable due to any unreasonable restriction of time, 
geographical area, scope of activity, or otherwise, in lieu of declaring such 
provision
unenforceable, the court, to the extent permissible by law, shall, at the 
Employer&#146;s request revise or reconstruct such provisions in a manner 
sufficient to cause them to be enforceable. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; 
font-family:Times New Roman">25. <U>Confidentiality</U>. The Executive 
acknowledges and agrees that the terms and conditions and the financial details 
of this Agreement
are confidential, and the Executive agrees that he will not disclose the same to
non-parties under any circumstances unless compelled by law. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; 
font-family:Times New Roman">26. <U>Injunctive Relief</U>. The Executive 
acknowledges that a remedy at law for any breach or threatened breach of 
Section&nbsp;7 or 8 of
this Agreement will be inadequate and that Employer shall be entitled to 
specific performance, injunctive relief, and any other remedies available to it 
for such breach or threatened breach. If a bond is required to be posted in 
order for Employer
to secure an injunction, then the Parties stipulate that a bond in the amount of
One Thousand and No/100 Dollars (US$1,000) will be sufficient and reasonable in 
all circumstances to protect the rights of the Parties. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; 
font-family:Times New Roman">27. <U>Section&nbsp;409A</U>. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; 
font-family:Times New Roman">(a) To the extent applicable, this Agreement shall 
be interpreted and administered in a manner so that any amount or benefit 
payable shall be
paid or provided in a manner that is either exempt from or compliant with the 
requirements of Section&nbsp;409A of the Internal Revenue Code of 1986, as 
amended, and applicable guidance and regulations issued
</P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P 
STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New

Executive Employment Agreement </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt;
font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="right">Page 12 </P>
<p Style='page-break-before:always'>

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times 
New Roman">
thereunder (&#147;<U>Section 409A</U>&#148;). The parties agree to work together
in good faith in an effort to comply with Section&nbsp;409A and any provision 
that would cause this Agreement to
fail to satisfy Section&nbsp;409A shall have no force and effect until amended 
to comply therewith (which amendment may be retroactive to the extent permitted 
by Section&nbsp;409A). In addition, for purposes of this Agreement, each amount 
to be paid
or benefit to be provided to the Executive pursuant to this Agreement shall be 
construed as a separate identified payment for purposes of Section&nbsp;409A. 
</P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; 
font-family:Times New Roman">(b) With respect to any amount of expenses eligible
for reimbursement under this Agreement, such expenses shall be reimbursed by the
Company
within thirty (30)&nbsp;days following the date on which the Company receives 
the applicable documentation from the Executive in accordance with its expense 
reimbursement policies, but in no event later than the last day of the 
Executive&#146;s
taxable year following the taxable year in which the Executive incurs the 
related expenses. In no event shall the reimbursements or in-kind benefits to be
provided under this Agreement in one taxable year affect the amount of 
reimbursements or
in-kind benefits to be provided in any other taxable year, nor will the 
Executive&#146;s right to reimbursement or in-kind benefits be subject to 
liquidation or exchange for another benefit. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; 
font-family:Times New Roman">(c) Notwithstanding any provision to the contrary 
in this Agreement, if the Executive is deemed as of the Executive&#146;s 
Termination Date to
be a &#147;Specified Employee&#148; within the meaning of that term under Code 
Section&nbsp;409A(a)(2)(B), then with regard to any payment or the provision of 
any benefit that is required to be delayed in compliance with Code
Section&nbsp;409A(a)(2)(B), such payment or benefit (the &#147;Delayed 
Payment&#148;) shall not be made or provided prior to the earlier of 
(i)&nbsp;the first business day of the seventh month measured from the date of 
the Executive&#146;s
separation from service (within the meaning of Section&nbsp;409A or 
(ii)&nbsp;the date of the Executive&#146;s death (the &#147;<U>Delay 
Period</U>&#148;). Upon the expiration of the Delay Period (the 
&#147;<U>Permissible Payment Date</U>&#148;),
all Delayed Payments (whether they would have otherwise been payable in a single
sum or in installments in the absence of such delay) shall be paid or reimbursed
to the Executive in a lump sum on the Permissible Payment Date, and any 
remaining
payments and benefits due under this Agreement shall be paid or provided in 
accordance with the normal payment dates specified for them herein. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; 
font-family:Times New Roman">28. <U>Counsel</U>. The Executive acknowledges that
he is executing a legal document that contains certain duties, obligations and
restrictions as specified herein. The Executive furthermore acknowledges that he
has been advised of his right to retain legal counsel, and that he has either 
been represented by legal counsel prior to his execution hereof or has knowingly
elected
not to be so represented. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; 
text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">By signing below, 
the Executive acknowledges that he has received, read, and agrees to adhere to 
the terms and
conditions contained within this Agreement. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt;

 <BODY BGCOLOR="WHITE">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times 
New Roman" ALIGN="right"><B>Exhibit 10.5 </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times 
New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B><U>AMENDED AND RESTATED EXECUTIVE EMPLOYMENT 
AGREEMENT </U></B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times 
New Roman">THIS AMENDED AND RESTATED EXECUTIVE EMPLOYMENT AGREEMENT (the 
&#147;<U>Agreement</U>&#148;), effective as of the Effective Date (as defined 
below), is entered
into by and between SAExploration Holdings, Inc., a Delaware corporation (the 
&#147;<U>Employer</U>&#148; or the &#147;<U>Company</U>&#148;), and <U>Darin 
Silvernagle</U>, an individual residing in the Province of Alberta, Canada (the
&#147;<U>Executive</U>&#148;) and amends, restates and replaces in its entirety 
the Executive Employment Agreement dated as of January&nbsp;1, 2014, other than 
the provisions of the Non-Disclosure Agreement (as such term is defined herein) 
(the
&#147;<U>Original Employment Agreement</U>&#148;). The Employer and the 
Executive may be referred to singularly as &#147;<U>Party</U>&#148; or 
collectively as &#147;<U>Parties</U>.&#148; Unless otherwise specified, 
capitalized terms have the
meanings set forth herein. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:24pt; margin-bottom:0pt; 
font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><U>RECITALS </U></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; 
font-family:Times New Roman">WHEREAS, the Company and certain of its 
subsidiaries and such other parties identified therein entered into that certain
Restructuring Support
Agreement dated as of June&nbsp;13, 2016, whereby the parties thereto have 
agreed to enter into certain transactions that will have the effect of 
restructuring and recapitalizing the Company (the &#147;<U>RSA</U>&#148;) 
effective upon the Closing
Date (as such term is defined in the RSA); </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; 
margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New 
Roman">WHEREAS, prior to the Effective Date, the Employer has employed the 
Executive as Executive
Vice President&#151;Marine of the Company; </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; 
margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New 
Roman">WHEREAS, in connection with and pursuant to the provisions of the RSA, 
the Parties have agreed
to amend the Original Employment Agreement on the terms and conditions contained
herein effective immediately upon the date of approval (the &#147;<U>Effective 
Date</U>&#148;) by the Board of Directors of the Company (the 
&#147;<U>Board</U>&#148;);
</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-
size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">WHEREAS, effective immediately upon the 
Effective Date, the Company will employ the Executive as the Vice 
President&#151;Marine of the
Company, and the Executive desires to be employed by the Employer on the terms 
and conditions contained herein; </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-
bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New 
Roman">WHEREAS, the Employer
acknowledges and rewards the value and loyalty of the Executive and seeks to 
build and protect the Company&#146;s stability, growth, customer base, 
technology and other competitive advantages; and </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; 
font-family:Times New Roman">WHEREAS, the Executive wishes to evidence his 
commitment to the Company and its objectives. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; 
font-family:Times New Roman">NOW, THEREFORE, in consideration of the foregoing 
premises and the respective agreements hereinafter set forth and the mutual 
benefits to be
derived hereinafter, the Employer and the Executive hereby agree as follows: 
</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:24pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-
family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><U>AGREEMENTS </U></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; 
font-family:Times New Roman">1. <U>Employment Term</U>. The Employer hereby 
agrees to continue to employ the Executive commencing on the Effective Date and 
ending on the
third anniversary thereafter (the &#147;<U>Initial Term</U>&#148;); 
<U>provided</U>, <U>however</U>, that at the end of the Initial Term, the 
Executive&#146;s </P>
<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times 
New Roman">
employment and this Agreement shall automatically renew or extend for 
consecutive terms of one (1)&nbsp;year on each succeeding anniversary of the 
Effective Date (each such renewal or extension a
&#147;<U>Renewal Term</U>&#148;), unless either Party gives prior written notice
to the other Party of its desire to terminate the Agreement at least 90 days 
prior to the expiration of the Initial Term or any Renewal Term, as applicable 
(the Initial
Term and each Renewal Term, collectively, the &#147;<U>Term</U>&#148;). 
Notwithstanding the foregoing, the Parties shall have the termination rights as 
set forth in Section&nbsp;5 of this Agreement. Termination of this Agreement for
any reason
whatsoever by any Party shall have no effect on the continued enforceability of 
any ancillary agreement, specifically including the Non-Disclosure Agreement 
executed by the Executive in favor of the Employer concurrently with the
Original Employment
Agreement, (the &#147;<U>Non-Disclosure Agreement</U>&#148;). The obligations of
the Parties under Sections 5 through 27 shall survive according to the terms of 
each provision. The Executive accepts such continued employment and agrees to 
continue
to perform the services specified herein, all upon the terms and conditions 
hereinafter stated. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-
indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">2. <U>Duties</U>. During
the Term, the
Executive shall serve in the position of Vice President&#151;Marine of the 
Company and shall report to and be subject to the general direction and control 
of the Chief Executive Officer of the Company (the &#147;<U>CEO</U>&#148;) or 
the CEO&#146;s
designee. In such capacity he shall be responsible for the supervision of the 
day to day operations of the Company and the implementation of its business 
plans and strategies, in each case, subject to the CEO and in accordance with 
and subject to
budgets approved from time to time by such CEO. The Executive shall perform such
duties consistent with the Executive&#146;s position, as well as other duties 
from time to time assigned to the Executive by the CEO. The Executive further 
agrees to
perform, without additional compensation, such other services for the Employer 
and for any of its affiliates as the Board shall from time to time specify, if 
such services are of the nature commonly associated with or similar to that of 
the
Executive&#146;s position with a company engaged in activities similar to the 
activities engaged in by the Employer at the time of execution of this 
Agreement. For purposes of the Non-Disclosure Agreement and Sections 5 through 
27, the term
&#147;Employer&#148; shall be deemed to include and refer to any and all 
affiliates of the Employer. The Executive acknowledges and agrees that the Non-
Disclosure Agreement executed simultaneously with the Original Employment 
Agreement is hereby
incorporated by reference herein and made a part hereof and that the Non-
Disclosure Agreement constitutes a material part of this Agreement. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; 
font-family:Times New Roman">3. <U>Extent of Service</U>. The Executive shall 
devote his full business time, attention, and energy to the business of the 
Employer, and
shall not be engaged in any other business activity that competes with or 
detracts from the business of the Employer during the Term of this Agreement. 
The foregoing shall not be construed as preventing the Executive from making 
passive investments
in other businesses or enterprises, if (i)&nbsp;such investments will not 
require services on the part of the Executive which would in any material way 
impair the performance of his duties under this Agreement, or (ii)&nbsp;such 
other businesses or
enterprises are not engaged in any business competitive with the business of the
Employer or any of its affiliates. The Executive shall be based in the vicinity 
of the Calgary metropolitan area (or such other area as may be agreed upon by 
the
Parties) and, subject to travel requirements as reasonably necessary to support 
successful business development efforts and management of the business, shall 
perform his services from a mutually agreed location in that area. </P>

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt;
font-family:Times New Roman">4. <U>Compensation and Benefits</U>. As payment for
the services to be rendered by the Executive
hereunder during the Term of this Agreement, the Executive shall be entitled to 
the following: </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-
indent:8%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(a) receive payment of 
the
Executive&#146;s annual base salary at the rate of not less than US$291,818.00 a
year (the &#147;<U>Base Salary</U>&#148;), less deductions required by law, 
payable in accordance with the Employer&#146;s standard payroll schedule, but 
not less
frequently than monthly; <U>provided</U>, that commencing with the 
Company&#146;s 2017 fiscal year, the Executive&#146;s Base Salary may be 
increased annually (but not decreased without the written consent of the 
Executive) in the discretion of the
Board; </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-
size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(b) a monthly automobile allowance of 
US$1,000 per month payable in accordance with the Employer&#146;s standard 
payroll schedule,
and which shall be subject to customary deductions and withholding; </P> <P 
STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; font-
family:Times New Roman">(c) continue to be eligible to participate in any short-
term and
long-term incentive compensation plans, annual bonus plans and such other 
management incentive programs or arrangements of the Company approved by the 
Board that are generally available to the Company&#146;s senior executives and 
continue to be
eligible to receive annual performance cash awards (&#147;<U>Annual Cash 
Awards</U>&#148;) at the rate of 40% to 60% of Base Salary (the &#147;<U>Target 
Percentage</U>&#148;), and the Executive will be entitled to a guaranteed 20% 
annual performance
cash award and as much as 60% if certain executive goals (the &#147;<U>Executive
Goals</U>&#148;) are reached as identified and approved by the Compensation 
Committee of the Board (the &#147;<U>Compensation Committee</U>&#148;), but not 
to exceed
the maximum award permissible under the applicable long-term incentive plan for 
such annual award; <U>provided</U>, that, at the option of the Compensation 
Committee, up to 50% of any Annual Cash Award payable to the Executive may be 
paid in shares
of the Company&#146;s common stock (which is in addition to any shares of the 
Company&#146;s common stock reserved for issuance under the SAExploration 
Holdings, Inc. 2016 Long-Term Incentive Plan, as may be amended, restated and 
supplemented from
time to time (the &#147;<U>Equity Incentive Plan</U>&#148;)); <U>provided</U>, 
<U>further</U>, that such Target Percentage will be applied to twelve 
(12)&nbsp;times the highest paid monthly base salary within the applicable 
calendar year. Commencing
with the Company&#146;s 2017 fiscal year, the Executive Goals will be set by the
Compensation Committee under the applicable long-term incentive plan for such 
annual award but in any event shall not exceed the maximum award permissible 
under such
applicable plan; </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-
indent:8%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(d) the Executive will 
be entitled to participate, on the same basis generally as other similarly 
situated employees of
the Company, in all benefits as may be offered by the Company from time to time;
</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-
size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(e) reimbursement of reasonable expenses
incurred by the
Executive in accordance with such expense reimbursement policies of the Company;
and </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-
size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(f) paid vacation of six (6)&nbsp;weeks 
per year.
</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-
size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(g) <U>Equity Compensation</U>. The
Executive shall be eligible to participate in the Equity Incentive Plan and such
other equity
incentive programs or arrangements of the Company approved by the Board that are
generally available to the Company&#146;s senior executives. The </P>

<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; 
font-family:Times New Roman">5. <U>Termination</U>. This Agreement and the 
Executive&#146;s employment with the Company may be terminated in accordance 
with this
Section&nbsp;5. The date upon which any such termination becomes effective shall
be deemed the &#147;Termination Date.&#148; </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; 
margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New 
Roman">(a)
<U>Termination by the Company for Cause</U>. The Company may terminate this 
Agreement and Executive&#146;s employment with the Company at any time without 
notice and without any payment to the Executive whatsoever, save and except for 
the payment of
any Base Salary, vacation accrued but unpaid up to the Termination Date and out 
of pocket expenses in accordance with Section&nbsp;4(e), if the Executive 
engages in any of the following conduct (termination for &#147;Cause&#148;): 
</P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:13%; font-size:10pt; 
font-family:Times New Roman">(i) the breaching of any material provision of this
Agreement after Company has given the Executive reasonable notice of such breach
and a
reasonable opportunity to correct, or cause to be corrected, such breach; </P> 
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:13%; font-size:10pt; 
font-family:Times New Roman">(ii) knowing and intentional misappropriation of 
funds or
property of the Company or its affiliates; </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; 
margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:13%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New 
Roman">(iii) engaging in conduct, even if not in connection with the performance
of the duties
hereunder, which might be reasonably expected to result in any effect materially
adverse to the interests of the Company or any of its affiliates, such as fraud,
dishonesty, conviction (or a judicial finding of evidence sufficient to convict)
of any
felony; </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P 
STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:13%; font-size:10pt;

assigned to the Executive in accordance with the
terms hereto after the Company has given the Executive reasonable notice of such
failure and a reasonable opportunity to correct, or cause to be corrected, such 
failure; </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:13%; font-size:10pt;

the Company or any of its affiliates that are promulgated from time to time by

<U>provided</U>, <U>however</U>, that the Company shall not be unreasonably

<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:13%; font-size:10pt;

<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:13%; font-size:10pt; 
font-family:Times New Roman">(vii) disability of the Executive which prevents 
the Executive from performing the essential functions of the position assigned 
under this
Agreement, with or without reasonable accommodation. Disability status under 
this Agreement will be consistent with the disability and leave procedures 
promulgated from time to time by the Company. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; 
font-family:Times New Roman">(b) <U>Termination by the Executive for Good 
Reason</U>. The Executive shall have good reason (&#147;<U>Good 
Reason</U>&#148;) as defined
below to resign his employment within sixty (60)&nbsp;days following notice and 
receive the payments as provided under Section&nbsp;6 (and subject to the same 
release requirement), provided the Executive has first provided written notice 
to the
Employer of conduct warranting termination of the Executive&#146;s employment 
for Good Reason and provided the Employer a period of not less than thirty 
(30)&nbsp;days to cure such conduct, without the written consent of the 
Executive: </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:13%; font-size:10pt; 
font-family:Times New Roman">(i) a material diminution in the nature and scope 
of the Executive&#146;s authorities or duties, including but not limited to a 
change in the
Executive&#146;s reporting relationship, a required move of more than a 50-mile 
radius of the Executive&#146;s employment prior to any such relocation, except 
for reasonably required travel on the Company&#146;s business or a reduction in 
pay (which
shall not be triggered by the Company&#146;s setting of the Executive Goals, 
beginning with the Company&#146;s 2017 fiscal year, pursuant Section&nbsp;4(c) 
above, even if the Executive&#146;s Annual Cash Award payout decreases as a 
result); or </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:13%; font-size:10pt; 
font-family:Times New Roman">(ii) a material breach of this Agreement by the 
Employer. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; 
font-family:Times New Roman">(c) <U>Termination by the Executive Without Good 
Reason</U>. The Executive may terminate his employment with the Company at any 
time, for any
reason, by providing 60 days&#146; advance written notice to the Company, which 
may be waived in whole or in part by the Company. If the Company waives the 
notice period in whole or in part, the Company shall pay the Base Salary for the
portion of
the notice period that has been waived. The Executive shall only be entitled to 
payment of any accrued but unpaid Base Salary, accrued but unpaid out of pocket 
expenses in accordance with Section&nbsp;4(e) hereof and vacation pay accrued 
but unpaid
up to the Termination Date. The Executive shall not be entitled to any accrued 
annual bonus or other benefits. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-
bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(d) 
<U>Termination by the
Company Without Cause</U>. The Company may terminate the Executive&#146;s
employment without Cause. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; 
text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(e) <U>Termination 
by Change of
Control</U>. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P 
STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:13%; font-size:10pt; 
font-family:Times New Roman">(i) Subject to Section&nbsp;5(e)(ii) below, within 
six (6)&nbsp;months following a Change of
Control of the Company, should the Company not renew or replace this Agreement 
with an Agreement containing substantially the same or better terms, the 
Executive shall be entitled to receive termination payments as set out in 
Section&nbsp;6 (but
subject to the requirement of a full and final release in favor of the Company 
in a form satisfactory to the Company), except that the 15-day period payment 
shall not apply, but instead the payment shall be made as a single lump 
immediately
following the expiration of a six (6)&nbsp;month period from the date the 
Executive elected to terminate his employment with the Company. &#147;Change of 
Control&#148; shall mean such time as any of the following occur after the date 
of this
Agreement: (i)&nbsp;a tender offer or exchange offer is made and consummated for
the ownership of fifty-one percent (51%)&nbsp;of the outstanding voting 
securities of the Company, (ii)&nbsp;the Company is merged or consolidated with 
another entity
and as a result of such merger or consolidation fifty-one percent (51%)&nbsp;of 
the outstanding voting securities of the surviving or resulting entity is owned 
directly or indirectly in the aggregate by a person or persons other than a 
person or
persons who owned fifty one percent (51%)&nbsp;of the outstanding voting 
securities of the Company immediately prior to such merger or consolidation, 
(iii)&nbsp;the Company is liquidated or otherwise sells or transfers all or 
substantially all of
its assets to another entity which is not wholly owned, directly or indirectly, 
by a person or persons who own fifty percent (50%)&nbsp;or more of the 
outstanding voting securities of the Company, or (iv)&nbsp;a person, within the 
meaning of
Section&nbsp;3(a)(9) or Section&nbsp;13(d)(3) of the Securities Exchange Act of 
1934, as amended and in effect from time to time, acquires over fifty one 
percent (51%)&nbsp;or more of the outstanding voting securities of the Company 
(whether
directly, indirectly, beneficially or of record). </P> <P STYLE="margin-
top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:13%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times 
New Roman">(ii) Notwithstanding Section&nbsp;5(e)(i) hereof to the contrary, the
Executive
acknowledges and agrees that the Executive has waived such provision and the 
corresponding provision under Section&nbsp;5(d) of the Original Employment 
Agreement and any right to claim any such compensation and benefits provided 
under this Agreement
in connection therewith with respect to the transactions specified in the RSA 
(the &#147;<U>Restructuring Transactions</U>&#148;), and further acknowledges 
and agrees that the Restructuring Transactions shall not be considered a Change 
of Control
under this Section&nbsp;5(e) or under Section&nbsp;5(d) of the Original 
Employment Agreement. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-
indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">6. <U>Payments Upon 
Termination</U>. In the
event this Agreement and the Executive&#146;s employment with the Company is 
terminated by the Executive with Good Reason under Section&nbsp;5(b), by the 
Company without Cause under Section&nbsp;5(d) or by the Executive under the 
circumstances
described under Section&nbsp;5(e), the Executive shall be entitled to: </P> <P 
STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; font-

Termination Date;
</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-
size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(b) all accrued but unpaid vacation pay 
to the Termination Date; </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; 
font-family:Times New Roman">(c) payment equal to twenty-four 
(24)&nbsp;months&#146; Base Salary; </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; 
font-family:Times New Roman">(d) payment equal to the previous two 
(2)&nbsp;years&#146; bonuses paid to the Executive, plus a prorated portion of 
any bonus for the year of
the Executive&#146;s termination in an amount as provided under the applicable 
bonus plan of the Company, assuming a payment at the Target Percentage of 100%. 
If a bonus payment was not paid to the Executive in any of those previous two
(2)&nbsp;years, the amount for this section will be calculated on the assumption
that the bonus paid for any unpaid year was paid at the Target Percentage of 
100%; and </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P 
STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New 
Roman" ALIGN="right">Amended and Restated
Executive Employment Agreement </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt;
font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="right">Page 7 </P>
<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; 
font-family:Times New Roman">(e) five percent (5%)&nbsp;of the amount paid 
pursuant to Section&nbsp;6(a) as compensation for
the loss of employment benefits. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-
bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Prior to, and as a 
condition to, receiving the payments in Section&nbsp;6 (other than payments 
pursuant to Sections 6(a)
and (b)), the Executive agrees to execute a full and final release in favor of 
the Company, in a form satisfactory to the Company, not later than fifteen 
(15)&nbsp;days following the Termination Date. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times 
New Roman">The above amounts will be paid in a single lump sum not later than 
fifteen (15)&nbsp;days of the Termination Date subject to the fulfillment of the
provision
of a full and final release,<U> provided</U>, <U>however</U>, if such 15-day 
period begins in one taxable year and ends in a second taxable year, the payment
date shall be deemed to be the later of (i)&nbsp;the first business day in the 
year
following the year in which the Executive&#146;s &#147;separation from 
service&#148; occurs or (ii)&nbsp;the last day of such 15-day period. The 
payments referred to in this Section&nbsp;6 shall not be subject to the 
requirement of mitigation, nor
reduced by any actual mitigation by the Executive and are inclusive of any 
termination and/or severance payments that may be required under employment 
standards legislation. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; 
font-family:Times New Roman">7. <U>Non-Disclosure/Confidentiality 
Obligations</U>. The parties contemplate the Executive providing executive 
services to the Company in
connection with its core business of providing effective acquisition of seismic 
data (the &#147;<U>Business</U>&#148;). To facilitate the Executive&#146;s
ability to perform these services, the Company agrees to provide the Executive 
confidential,
proprietary, trade secret information regarding the Company&#146;s business 
strategies, plans, techniques and processes, which are more fully set forth in 
the Non-Disclosure Agreement (&#147;<U>Confidential Information</U>&#148;), 
which the Company
uses to compete in the marketplace, and the Executive agrees not to use or 
disclose such Confidential Information for any purpose other than to advance the
Company&#146;s interests. Moreover, from time to time, subsidiary companies or 
affiliates of
the Company may provide that entity&#146;s confidential, proprietary information
which the Company uses to compete in the marketplace, to the Executive to 
facilitate the Executive&#146;s ability to provide services to the subsidiary 
companies or
affiliates, and the Executive agrees not to use or disclose such Confidential 
Information for any purpose other than to advance the subsidiary companies&#146;
or affiliate&#146;s interests. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; 
font-family:Times New Roman">8. <U>Post-Employment Obligations</U>. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; 
font-family:Times New Roman">During the Term of this Agreement and for 12 months
following the Termination Date: </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; 
font-family:Times New Roman">(a) the Executive will not, as a competitor or on 
behalf of any competitor of the Company, directly or indirectly solicit or 
accept Business
from any Customer (as defined in the Non-Disclosure Agreement): (i)&nbsp;with 
whom the Executive had contact as a result of his duties with the Company or its
affiliates, and/or (ii)&nbsp;about whom the Executive reviewed or obtained 
Confidential
Information (as defined in the Non-Disclosure Agreement) while performing 
services for the Company or its affiliates. The geographic limitation for this 
restriction is (1)&nbsp;any Company or its affiliates&#146; territory in which 
the Executive had
a customer or </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P 
STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New

New Roman">
service assignment for the Company or its affiliates in the twelve 
(12)&nbsp;month period immediately preceding the Executive&#146;s Termination 
Date; and/or (2)&nbsp;any territory in which the
Company or its affiliates, have customers or service assignments about which the
Executive obtained Confidential Information during the term of this Agreement; 
and </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; 
font-family:Times New Roman">(b) the Executive will not solicit, induce or 
attempt to induce any other employee, agent or contractor of the Company or its 
affiliates with
whom the Executive worked or about whom the Executive obtained Confidential

Executive&#146;s Termination Date, to leave the employ of the Company or its

for a competitor of the Company or its affiliates in the same or similar 
capacity as the other employee, agent or contractor of the Company or its 
affiliates worked for the Company or its affiliates. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt;
font-family:Times New Roman">(c) At the option of the Company, and in its sole 
discretion, the Company on the Termination Date may elect to extend the 
provisions of
Section&nbsp;8(a) and (b)&nbsp;for an additional twelve (12)&nbsp;months, in 
which case, the Company will pay to the Executive an amount equal to twelve 
(12)&nbsp;months of Base Salary as in effect at the Termination Date plus the 
Executive&#146;s
annual performance cash award under Section&nbsp;4(c) hereof at the 
Executive&#146;s Target Percentage of 50%, which shall be paid at the same time 
as the lump sum cash payment is made pursuant to Section&nbsp;6, as applicable, 
or, in the absence of
such a payment, within 15 days following the Termination Date, in exchange for

OTHER PROCEEDING WHICH SEEKS, IN WHOLE OR IN PART, TO CHALLENGE THE VALIDITY OR
ENFORCEABILITY OF THIS AGREEMENT OR ANY PROVISION HEREOF. THIS WAIVER SHALL 
APPLY TO ANY SUBSEQUENT AMENDMENTS, RENEWALS, SUPPLEMENTS OR MODIFICATIONS TO 
THIS AGREEMENT. </P>

font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">27. <U>Section&nbsp;409A</U>. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; 
font-family:Times New Roman">(a) To the extent applicable, this Agreement shall 
be interpreted and administered in a manner so that any amount or benefit 
payable shall be
paid or provided in a manner that is either exempt from or compliant with the 
requirements of Section&nbsp;409A of the Internal Revenue Code of 1986, as 
amended, and applicable guidance and regulations issued thereunder 
(&#147;<U>Section
409A</U>&#148;). The parties agree to work together in good faith in an effort 
to comply with Section&nbsp;409A and any provision that would cause this 
Agreement to fail to satisfy Section&nbsp;409A shall have no force and effect 
until amended to
comply therewith (which amendment may be retroactive to the extent permitted by 
Section&nbsp;409A). In addition, for purposes of this Agreement, each amount to 
be paid or benefit to be provided to the Executive pursuant to this Agreement 
shall be
construed as a separate identified payment for purposes of Section&nbsp;409A. 
</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-
size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(b) With respect to any amount of 
expenses eligible for
reimbursement under this Agreement, such expenses shall be reimbursed by the 
Company within thirty (30)&nbsp;days following the date on which the Company 
receives the applicable documentation from the Executive in accordance with its 
expense
reimbursement policies, but in no event later than the last day of the
Executive&#146;s taxable year following the taxable year in which the Executive 
incurs the related expenses. In no event shall the reimbursements or in-kind 
benefits to be
provided under this Agreement in one taxable year affect the amount of 
reimbursements or in-kind benefits to be provided in any other taxable year, nor
will the Executive&#146;s right to reimbursement or in-kind benefits be subject 
to liquidation or
exchange for another benefit. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt;
text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(c) Notwithstanding
any provision to the contrary in this Agreement, if the Executive is deemed as 
of the
Executive&#146;s Termination Date to be a &#147;Specified Employee&#148; within 
the meaning of that term under Code Section&nbsp;409A(a)(2)(B), then with regard
to any payment or the provision of any benefit that is required to be delayed in
compliance with Code Section&nbsp;409A(a)(2)(B), such payment or benefit (the 
&#147;Delayed Payment&#148;) shall not be made or provided prior to the earlier 
of (i)&nbsp;the first business day of the seventh month measured from the date 
of the
Executive&#146;s separation from service (within the meaning of 
Section&nbsp;409A or (ii)&nbsp;the date of the Executive&#146;s death (the 
&#147;<U>Delay Period</U>&#148;). Upon the expiration of the Delay Period (the 
&#147;<U>Permissible Payment
Date</U>&#148;), all Delayed Payments (whether they would have otherwise been 
payable in a single sum or in installments in the absence of such delay) shall 
be paid or reimbursed to the Executive in a lump sum on the Permissible Payment 
Date, and
any remaining payments and benefits due under this Agreement shall be paid or 
provided in accordance with the normal payment dates specified for them herein.
